# TLICA → `brain/` Invariant Catalog (v0.31)

This catalog is the spine of the v0 plan. Each row binds a Lean source declaration in `lean-scratch-main/TLICA/` to a Python runtime check in `brain/`, names the owning Python module, and points at the fixture that exercises it. v0's success criterion is: every row marked **REQUIRED** asserts green on its named fixture under the deterministic stubs.

> **Catalog version:** v0.35. Patches over v0.34 (Phase 3.26 Active Hypothesis + Self-Directed Probe Loop): +13 REQUIRED rows, +1 STRUCTURAL row, OBSERVED unchanged, NOT-EXERCISED unchanged, DEFERRED unchanged. Adds the `I-AHYP-01..I-AHYP-14` row family covering one new module `brain/development/active_hypothesis_probe.py` (pure bounded deterministic OFFLINE live-test runner with the closed `AmbiguityCondition` 5-value enum, the closed `ActiveHypothesisStatus` 4-value enum, the closed `ProbeConstructionRule` 6-value enum, the closed `TrialVerdict` 4-value enum, the closed `ProbeOutcome` 2-value enum, and the bounded `ActiveHypothesisCandidate`, `ActiveProbeStep`, `ActiveHypothesisTrial`, `ActiveHypothesisResult`, `ActiveHypothesisLiveTestReport` records). The new module exposes `enumerate_hypotheses`, `select_safe_probe`, `construct_probe_text`, `run_active_hypothesis_trial`, `run_active_hypothesis_live_test`, `format_active_hypothesis_live_test_report`, `active_hypothesis_live_test_digest`, plus a `python3 -m brain.development.active_hypothesis_probe` direct runner. The runner probes whether the existing substrate realizes the operational analogue of *active hypothesis + self-directed probe*: given a bounded ambiguous structural input, the runtime enumerates a bounded candidate set, selects one safe internal probe per candidate (no expected-outcome leak), executes the probe via `run_agent_interaction_step`, prunes candidates whose observed probe digest does not match the candidate's `predicted_digest_hex16`, declines to nominate a winner when zero candidates survive, and on a second invocation against the same cache reuses the prior surviving record without re-probing. Five bounded conditions: `CONTROL_NO_AMBIGUITY`, `SINGLE_HYPOTHESIS_CONVERGES`, `MULTI_HYPOTHESIS_NARROWS`, `NO_HYPOTHESIS_SURVIVES`, `REUSE_CACHED_HYPOTHESIS`. The v1 ten-trial battery covers shapes A B A / A B B / A B C / A B A B / A A / A A B; the live-test report produces a deterministic 16-hex digest stable across two fresh runs (`86b67d97daeb251d` on the v1 plan). The benchmark battery adds one axis: A13 `active_hypothesis` (14 cases A13.01–A13.14). Total benchmark cases: 105 (91 from Phase 3.22 / 3.22b / 3.23 / 3.24 / 3.25 + 14 from Phase 3.26); 104 PASS + 1 documented WARN (A3.04, the Phase 3.21 W3 follow-up blocker, unchanged) + 0 FAIL. Closed import set for the new module: no `brain.llm`, no `brain.tick`, no `brain.ui`, no curses, no `os` / `subprocess` / `socket` / `urllib` / `http` / `requests` / `pathlib` / `tempfile` / `shutil` / `threading` / `asyncio` / `atexit` / `signal` / `importlib` / `time` / `random` / `math` import; the new module uses `hashlib` only at the digest-construction boundary. The runtime path of every probe step NEVER receives the candidate's `predicted_digest_hex16` or `predicted_shape`; expected-outcome labels live only on the `ActiveHypothesisTrial` record and are used exclusively by the benchmark-assertion layer after `run_active_hypothesis_trial` returns. Operator inputs (input texts and constructed probe texts) are scanned for forbidden direct-instruction terms (`learn`, `remember`, `pattern`, `classify`, `transfer`, `reuse`, `abab`, `abba`, `abcabc`, `structure`, `shape`, `imprint`, `osmotic`, `absorb`, `imbibe`, `intuition`, `hypothesis`, `candidate`, `probe`, `predict`, `falsify`, `survive`, `decide`, `infer`, `wonder`); the v1 battery uses none of them in operator-input text. The Phase 3.26 patch does NOT introduce any new `GrowthEventType`, any new `GrowthEventSource`, any new `OperatorCommand`, any new `LOCAL_COMMAND_VERBS` entry, any new `ACTIVE_VIEWS` value, any new `LearningEvidenceKind` member, any new `ReasoningStepKind` member, any new aggregate scalar field (no "hypothesis confidence score", no "active inquiry score", no "I-ness score"), any new dispatcher kind, any new operator verb, any new persistence schema, any new autosave trigger, any new TLICA runtime mutation, any kernel surface change, any L1 / L2 cache semantic change, any parser change, any prompt change, any Pattern Ledger / Coherence Monitor / Growth Ledger semantic change, any SelfModel implementation, or any consciousness / sentience / subjective / semantic / truth / agency / self-modification / introspection / metacognition / desire / will / belief / understanding / perception / world / embodiment / intuition / unconscious-learning / real-hypothesis-formation / real-inquiry / real-curiosity / real-deliberation / real-decision-making / real-planning claim. "Active hypothesis" / "self-directed probe" is a controlled technical metaphor for *bounded structural candidate enumeration + falsification + caching at the substrate level*; it is engineering shorthand and does NOT claim psychological hypothesis formation, inquiry, deliberation, decision-making, planning, introspection, metacognition, or any cognitive property of the running system. "Self-directed" means the probe text is derived from the input by a closed deterministic rule; it does NOT mean the runtime has a goal, plan, will, or any cognitive process. The two phases (enumerate-then-probe and falsify-then-cache) are distinct, transverse to the four imprinting kinds and to the Phase 3.25 osmotic imprinting+activation surface, and substrate-level only. No existing fixture is renamed. `brain/.llm_cache/` remains gitignored. The TLICA Lean spec in `lean_reference/` is not contradicted: every new row is marked as Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3 source label), no Lean theorem is claimed, no existing REQUIRED row is modified. v0.34 history retained (Phase 3.25 Osmotic Learning Live Test): +13 REQUIRED rows, +1 STRUCTURAL row, OBSERVED unchanged, NOT-EXERCISED unchanged, DEFERRED unchanged. Adds the `I-OSMO-01..I-OSMO-14` row family covering one new module `brain/development/osmotic_learning_probe.py` (pure bounded deterministic OFFLINE live-test runner with the closed `OsmoticCondition` 4-value enum and the closed `OsmoticProbeStatus` 4-value enum and the bounded `OsmoticExposureEvent`, `OsmoticProbeTrial`, `OsmoticProbeResult`, `OsmoticLiveTestReport` records). The new module exposes `build_osmotic_exposure_plan`, `run_osmotic_probe_trial`, `run_osmotic_live_test`, `format_osmotic_live_test_report`, and `osmotic_live_test_digest`, plus a `python3 -m brain.development.osmotic_learning_probe` direct runner. The runner probes whether the existing substrate (abstract_pattern signature + learning evidence + reasoning trace + dispatch trace) realizes the operational analogue of osmotic imprinting (ambient unlabeled exposure creates a session-local `ABSTRACT_PATTERN_ACQUIRED` record) and activation (a later renamed / transformed probe with the same abstract digest re-activates the record via `ABSTRACT_PATTERN_REUSED` + `TRANSFER_RECOGNIZED`) under four bounded conditions: CONTROL_NO_EXPOSURE, TRUE_EXPOSURE, SHAM_EXPOSURE, DISTRACTOR_INTERFERENCE. The v1 ten-trial battery covers ABAB, ABBA, AAB, ABCABC target shapes; the live-test report produces a deterministic 16-hex digest stable across two fresh runs (`7aa91075cd76ea73` on the v1 plan). The benchmark battery adds one axis: A12 `osmotic_learning` (14 cases A12.01–A12.14). Total benchmark cases: 91 (77 from Phase 3.22 / 3.22b / 3.23 / 3.24 + 14 from Phase 3.25); 90 PASS + 1 documented WARN (A3.04, the Phase 3.21 W3 follow-up blocker, unchanged) + 0 FAIL. Closed import set for the new module: no `brain.llm`, no `brain.tick`, no `brain.ui`, no curses, no `os` / `subprocess` / `socket` / `urllib` / `http` / `requests` / `pathlib` / `tempfile` / `shutil` / `threading` / `asyncio` / `atexit` / `signal` / `importlib` / `time` / `random` / `math` import; the new module uses `hashlib` only at the digest-construction boundary. The runtime path of every probe trial NEVER receives the expected target digest or expected shape; expected-shape labels live only on the `OsmoticProbeTrial` record and are used exclusively by the benchmark-assertion layer after `run_osmotic_probe_trial` returns. Exposure and probe texts are scanned for forbidden direct-instruction terms (`learn`, `remember`, `pattern`, `classify`, `transfer`, `reuse`, `ABAB`, `ABBA`, `ABCABC`, `structure`, `shape`, `imprint`, `osmotic`, `absorb`, `imbibe`, `intuition`); the v1 battery uses none of them in operator-input text. The Phase 3.25 patch does NOT introduce any new `GrowthEventType`, any new `GrowthEventSource`, any new `OperatorCommand`, any new `LOCAL_COMMAND_VERBS` entry, any new `ACTIVE_VIEWS` value, any new aggregate scalar field (no "consciousness score", no "sentience score", no "awareness score", no "I-ness score", no "learning score", no "osmotic absorption score"), any new dispatcher kind, any new operator verb, any new persistence schema, any new autosave trigger, any new TLICA runtime mutation, any kernel surface change, any L1 / L2 cache semantic change, any parser change, any prompt change, any Pattern Ledger / Coherence Monitor / Growth Ledger semantic change, any SelfModel implementation, or any consciousness / sentience / subjective / semantic / truth / agency / self-modification / introspection / metacognition / desire / will / belief / understanding / perception / world / embodiment / intuition / unconscious-learning claim. "Osmotic learning" / "osmotic imprinting" is a controlled technical metaphor for *unlabeled exposure-driven structural uptake at the substrate level*; it is engineering shorthand and does NOT claim psychological learning, intuition, awareness, or any cognitive property of the running system. "Imprinting" means formation of a substrate pattern (the `ABSTRACT_PATTERN_ACQUIRED` record); "activation" means later operational triggering / reuse (the `ABSTRACT_PATTERN_REUSED` + `TRANSFER_RECOGNIZED` records); the two phases are distinct, transverse to the four imprinting kinds, and substrate-level only. No existing fixture is renamed. `brain/.llm_cache/` remains gitignored. The TLICA Lean spec in `lean_reference/` is not contradicted: every new row is marked as Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3 source label), no Lean theorem is claimed, no existing REQUIRED row is modified.

> **Catalog version (prior):** v0.33. Patches over v0.32 (Phase 3.24 Worldlet Feedback Bridge): +11 REQUIRED rows, +1 STRUCTURAL row, OBSERVED unchanged, NOT-EXERCISED unchanged, DEFERRED unchanged. Adds the `I-WFDBK-01..I-WFDBK-12` row family covering one new bounded pure helper `build_worldlet_summary_text(...)` in `brain/development/processing_window.py`, two new `FeedbackMode` members `WORLDLET` and `PATTERN_COHERENCE_WORLDLET`, one new `InternalEventSource` member `WORLDLET_SUMMARY`, one new `OperatorSession` helper method `_run_worldlet_feedback_step`, two new closed-enum extensions (`ReasoningStepKind.CHECK_WORLDLET_FEEDBACK`, `LearningEvidenceKind.WORLDLET_FEEDBACK_RECORDED`), three new bounded `AgentObservationSummary` fields (`worldlet_feedback_present`, `worldlet_summary_count`, `feedback_mode_value`), one new bounded `LearningProofReport.worldlet_feedback_recorded_count` field, one new bounded `ReasoningTraceReport.check_worldlet_feedback_count` field, and one new benchmark axis `BenchmarkAxis.WORLDLET_FEEDBACK` with twelve cases `A11.01..A11.12`. The session-level `_dispatch_trace_session_facts` now emits a bounded `("worldlet_summary_chunks", "<int>")` derived fact. The processing window's `_run_processing_window` is widened to fire a deterministic `worldlet_summary` chunk after each rehearsal when `feedback_mode in {WORLDLET, PATTERN_COHERENCE_WORLDLET}`; the combined `PATTERN_COHERENCE_WORLDLET` mode fires `pledger_summary`, `cohmon_summary`, and `worldlet_summary` in the fixed order. The `worldlet_summary` chunk is produced by the new bounded pure helper that accepts only bounded primitives extracted from `OperatorSession.worldlet_history` (or the Phase 3.24 `"absent"` sentinel triple when no live worldlet history is present); the helper does NOT import `brain.development.worldlet` (mirroring the `pattern_ledger` and `coherence_monitor` decoupling precedents in `processing_window.py`). Total benchmark cases: 77 (65 from Phase 3.22 / 3.22b / 3.23 + 12 from Phase 3.24); 76 PASS + 1 documented WARN (A3.04 carry-over) + 0 FAIL. Closed import set for the helper and the new code remains unchanged: no `brain.llm`, no `brain.tick`, no curses, no `os` / `subprocess` / `socket` / `urllib` / `http` / `requests` / `pathlib` / `tempfile` / `shutil` / `threading` / `asyncio` / `atexit` / `signal` / `importlib` / `time` / `random` / `math` import; the new helper uses no `hashlib`, no random, no clock. The Phase 3.24 patch does NOT introduce any new `OperatorCommand`, any new `LOCAL_COMMAND_VERBS` entry, any new `ACTIVE_VIEWS` value, any new `GrowthEventType`, any new `GrowthEventSource`, any persistence schema column, any autosave trigger, any DB schema change, any L1 / L2 cache semantic change, any parser change, any prompt change, any Pattern Ledger / Coherence Monitor / Growth Ledger semantic change, any SelfModel implementation, any aggregate scalar field (no "consciousness score", no "world score", no "awareness score", no "I-ness score"), or any consciousness / sentience / subjective / semantic / truth / agency / self-modification / introspection / metacognition / desire / will / belief / understanding / perception / world / embodiment claim. "Worldlet feedback" is engineering shorthand for "a bounded structural summary of the session-local Minimal Worldlet substrate replayed through the processing window so the Pattern Ledger and downstream traces can observe it" -- never a claim of perception of an external world. The `I-AGENTLEARN-11`, `I-DTRACE-11`, and `I-DTRACE-12` rows are extended to acknowledge the closed-enum / slot extensions (one new value per enum, one new count field per report, the new bounded fields on `AgentObservationSummary`); no fixture file is renamed. `brain/.llm_cache/` remains gitignored. The TLICA Lean spec in `lean_reference/` is not contradicted: every new row is marked as Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3 source label), no Lean theorem is claimed, no existing REQUIRED row is modified.

> **Catalog version (prior):** v0.32. Patches over v0.31 (Phase 3.23 Dispatch Tracer Wiring): +11 REQUIRED rows, +1 STRUCTURAL row, OBSERVED unchanged, NOT-EXERCISED unchanged, DEFERRED unchanged. > **Catalog version (prior):** v0.31. Patches over v0.30 (Phase 3.22b Learning Evidence + Reasoning Trace Continuation): +10 REQUIRED rows, +1 STRUCTURAL row, OBSERVED unchanged, NOT-EXERCISED unchanged, DEFERRED unchanged. Adds the `I-AGENTLEARN-01..I-AGENTLEARN-11` row family across three new modules: `brain/development/abstract_pattern.py` (pure bounded structural-form layer), `brain/development/learning_evidence.py` (session-local evidence ledger with the closed `LearningEvidenceKind` enum and the bounded `LearningEvidenceRecord`, `LearningEvidenceTrace`, `LearningProofReport` records), and `brain/development/reasoning_trace.py` (closed audit trail with the `ReasoningStepKind` enum and bounded `ReasoningTraceStep`, `ReasoningTrace`, `ReasoningTraceReport` records). The agent loop is extended to populate `AgentLoopResult.learning_evidence_trace` and `AgentLoopResult.reasoning_trace` on every interaction. The benchmark battery adds two axes: A8 `learning_evidence` (7 cases A8.01–A8.07) and A9 `reasoning_trace` (7 cases A9.01–A9.07). Total benchmark cases: 53 (39 Phase 3.22 + 14 Phase 3.22b); 52 PASS + 1 documented WARN (A3.04, the Phase 3.21 W3 follow-up blocker) + 0 FAIL. Closed import set per new module: no `brain.llm`, no `brain.tick.tick`, no curses, no `os` / `subprocess` / `socket` / `urllib` / `http` / `requests` / `pathlib` / `tempfile` / `shutil` / `threading` / `asyncio` / `atexit` / `signal` / `importlib` / `time` / `random` / `math` import; the three new modules use `hashlib` only at digest-construction boundaries (mirroring `agent_benchmark.py` precedent). The W3 refusal trigger is refined: a narrower `_classify_cognitive_claim(text)` substring scan over a closed bounded tuple of phrase fragments (synthesized from the imported `_FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS` tuple) identifies direct cognitive-property phrasing for the reasoning trace; the wider audit-tuple scan remains the floor that fires REFUSAL. The W2 abstract-pattern transfer follow-up is satisfied by the new `derive_abstract_pattern_signature` layer: renamed inputs sharing structural form (e.g. "red blue red blue" and "cat dog cat dog") map to the same `digest_hex16` and trigger `TRANSFER_RECOGNIZED` evidence. The W5 REPL valid-effective follow-up is satisfied by the new `DIMINISHING_RETURNS_UPDATED` evidence kind which records the local-consequence DRF history. The W4 dispatch trace is satisfied by the reasoning trace's OBSERVE_INPUT step recording the dispatch-path label (one of `repl-bridge`, `session-dispatch-stream-append`, `refusal-no-dispatch`, `fail-no-dispatch`, `warn-no-dispatch`); the deterministic OFFLINE agent-loop path does not invoke `brain.tick.tick`. The Phase 3.22b patch does NOT introduce any new `GrowthEventType`, any new `GrowthEventSource`, any new `OperatorCommand`, any new `LOCAL_COMMAND_VERBS` entry, any new `ACTIVE_VIEWS` value, any new aggregate scalar field (no "consciousness score", no "sentience score", no "maturity score", no "intelligence score", no "capability score", no "I-ness score"), any new dispatcher kind, any new operator verb, any new persistence schema, any new autosave trigger, any new TLICA runtime mutation, any kernel surface change, any L1 / L2 cache semantic change, any parser change, any prompt change, any Pattern Ledger / Coherence Monitor / Growth Ledger semantic change, any SelfModel implementation, or any consciousness / sentience / subjective / semantic / truth / agency / self-modification / introspection / metacognition / desire / will / belief / understanding claim. "Structural learning" means observable session-local state transitions captured as bounded `LearningEvidenceRecord` rows — never memory in the psychological sense. "Reasoning trace" means an explicit audit trail of deterministic structural operations — never private subjective reasoning. The non-claim audit is the same `_FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS` tuple Phase 3.12c Coherence Monitor introduced; `I-AGENTLEARN-11` audits the three new module sources + `MODULE_PRODUCED_STRINGS` entries. `brain/.llm_cache/` remains gitignored. The TLICA Lean spec in `lean_reference/` is not contradicted: every new row is marked as Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3 source label), no Lean theorem is claimed, no existing REQUIRED row is modified.

> **Previous catalog version:** v0.30. Patches over v0.29 (Phase 3.22 Agent Communication Loop + Behavioral Indistinguishability Harness): +9 REQUIRED rows, +2 STRUCTURAL rows, OBSERVED unchanged, NOT-EXERCISED unchanged, DEFERRED unchanged. Adds the `I-AGENTLOOP-01..I-AGENTLOOP-11` row family across three new modules: `brain/development/agent_repl_bridge.py` (pure deterministic helpers over `brain/development/repl.py`), `brain/development/agent_loop.py` (bounded operator-facing reply layer composing Phase 3.18-3.21 substrates), and `brain/development/agent_benchmark.py` (closed deterministic seven-axis benchmark battery + runner module). Closed import set per module: no `brain.llm`, no `brain.tick.tick`, no curses, no `os` / `subprocess` / `socket` / `urllib` / `http` / `requests` / `pathlib` / `tempfile` / `shutil` / `threading` / `asyncio` / `atexit` / `signal` import; `agent_benchmark.py` additionally imports `hashlib` (transcript-digest computation at the runner boundary only) and `argparse` / `json` / `sys` (CLI surface). The agent loop module's source contains zero literal forbidden non-claim terms; the REFUSAL trigger reuses the imported `brain.development.coherence_monitor._FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS` tuple verbatim (case-insensitive substring) so any operator input containing a forbidden term routes to a closed REFUSAL reply that denies cognitive-property claims without using forbidden literals. Closed `AgentReplyStatus` `(str, Enum)` with exactly five members `PATTERN_REPORT`, `REPL_REPORT`, `COHERENCE_REPORT`, `LIMITATION_REPORT`, `NEXT_ACTION_SUGGESTION`; closed `AgentReplyDisposition` `(str, Enum)` with exactly four members `OK`, `REFUSAL`, `WARN`, `FAIL`; closed `BenchmarkAxis` `(str, Enum)` with exactly seven members `pattern_recognition`, `cross_input_structural`, `coherence_variation`, `repl_coherence`, `communication`, `session_continuity`, `blind_transcript`; closed `BenchmarkCaseStatus` `(str, Enum)` with `pass`, `warn`, `fail`. Frozen / slotted records `AgentInput`, `AgentObservationSummary`, `AgentReply`, `AgentLoopResult`, `AgentLoopState`, `AgentReplGrammarHandle`, `AgentReplLineResult`, `AgentReplBridgeSummary`, `BenchmarkCaseResult`, `AxisResult`, `BenchmarkRun` (every field bounded; no callable, no Fraction leakage upward, no mutable state). The full benchmark battery `run_full_battery()` runs 39 cases across the seven axes: 38 PASS + 1 documented WARN (A3.04 — overall-status `not_applicable` not publicly reachable because compute_overall_status returns NOT_APPLICABLE only when every check is NA but kernel.* checks always PASS for a valid BrainState; documented as the Phase 3.21 W3 follow-up blocker). The runner main `python3 -m brain.development.agent_benchmark` produces deterministic PASS / WARN / FAIL output (exit 0 PASS, 1 FAIL, 2 WARN-only), an optional JSON projection via `--json`, and a transcript digest computed as `sha256(joined_lines)[:16]` that is bit-identical across two runs. The deterministic battery consumes zero real model calls, zero cache writes, and produces zero forbidden-term hits. The Phase 3.22 patch does NOT introduce any new `GrowthEventType`, any new `GrowthEventSource`, any new `OperatorCommand`, any new `LOCAL_COMMAND_VERBS` entry, any new `ACTIVE_VIEWS` value, any new aggregate scalar field (no "mild-agent score", no "intelligence score", no "capability score", no "I-ness score"), any new dispatcher kind, any new operator verb, any new persistence schema, any new autosave trigger, any new TLICA runtime mutation, any kernel surface change, any L1 / L2 cache semantic change, any parser change, any prompt change, any Pattern Ledger / Coherence Monitor / Growth Ledger semantic change, any SelfModel implementation, or any consciousness / sentience / subjective / semantic / truth / agency / self-modification / introspection / metacognition / desire / will / belief / understanding claim. The word "agent" is used throughout in the **engineering** sense ("operator-facing agent loop"; "bounded agent reply") — never in the cognitive-agent or moral-agent sense. The Phase 3.22 acceptance criterion ("behaviorally mild-agent-like under bounded tests") is a closed-criterion property of the deterministic benchmark battery's outputs, NOT a cognitive claim. The non-claim audit is the same `_FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS` tuple Phase 3.12c Coherence Monitor introduced; `I-AGENTLOOP-10` audits agent_loop.py and agent_repl_bridge.py source + MODULE_PRODUCED_STRINGS, and `I-AGENTLOOP-11` audits agent_benchmark.py source + MODULE_PRODUCED_STRINGS. `brain/.llm_cache/` remains gitignored. The TLICA Lean spec in `lean_reference/` is not contradicted: every new row is marked as Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3 source label), no Lean theorem is claimed, no existing REQUIRED row is modified.

> **Previous catalog version:** v0.29. Patches over v0.28 (Phase 3.21 Developmental Trajectory): +10 REQUIRED rows, +1 STRUCTURAL row, OBSERVED unchanged, NOT-EXERCISED unchanged, DEFERRED unchanged. Adds the `I-DEVMILE-01..I-DEVMILE-11` row family at `brain/development/milestone_harness.py` for a bounded ten-milestone developmental-trajectory harness that is a strict consumer of the existing public surfaces. The harness defines a closed ten-member `DevelopmentalMilestone` `(str, Enum)` with members `M01_REFLEXIVE_BASELINE`, `M02_HABITUATION`, `M03_RECOGNITION`, `M04_REHEARSAL`, `M05_PATTERN_SELF_FEEDBACK`, `M06_STRUCTURAL_SELF_MONITORING`, `M07_MULTI_MODAL_INTEGRATION`, `M08_SATURATION_NOVELTY`, `M09_CROSS_INPUT_DIFFERENTIATION`, `M10_SUSTAINED_BEHAVIOR`; a closed four-member `MilestoneStatus` `(str, Enum)` with members `PASS`, `WARN`, `FAIL`, `NOT_APPLICABLE` (structural status labels only — never truth claims about the running system); a frozen / slotted `MilestoneResult` dataclass with exactly the five fields `milestone`, `status`, `summary`, `primary_metric`, `secondary_metric` (no aggregate scalar); ten pure deterministic per-milestone helpers `run_m01_*..run_m10_*` each constructing its own fresh `OperatorSession(state=initial_state(), ...)`, dispatching a bounded canonical input sequence through the public `STREAM_APPEND` path, computing the milestone's structural marker via inspection of `stream_history`, `pattern_ledger`, `growth_ledger`, and (for M06) `build_full_coherence_report`, running `assert_state_invariants(state)`, running the canonical `_FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS` audit over its produced summary string, and returning a frozen `MilestoneResult`; an aggregator `run_all_milestones()` returning a 10-tuple of `MilestoneResult` records in canonical order; bounded constants `MILESTONE_SUMMARY_MAX_LEN = 240` and a `MODULE_PRODUCED_STRINGS` tuple that contains every enum value and is audited against the canonical `_FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS` tuple. The harness import set is exactly `{__future__, dataclasses, enum, typing, brain.development.coherence_monitor (for build_full_coherence_report and _FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS), brain.development.growth_ledger (for GROWTH_LEDGER_MAX_EVENTS), brain.development.pattern_ledger (for derive_pattern_id / derive_pattern_signature), brain.development.processing_window (for FeedbackMode / PROCESSING_WINDOW_PROVENANCE_PREFIX), brain.development.text_stream (for STREAM_HISTORY_MAX_CHUNKS / STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_*), brain.tick (BrainState + initial_state + assert_state_invariants only — never the tick callable), brain.ui.commands (Command / OperatorCommand / StreamAppendPayload), brain.ui.session (OperatorSession), brain.tlica.profile (COGITO_ID)}`; no `brain.llm`, no curses, no `os` / `subprocess` / `socket` / `urllib` / `http` / `requests` / `pathlib` / `tempfile` / `shutil` / `threading` / `asyncio` / `atexit` / `signal` / `importlib` / `time` / `random` / `hashlib` / `math` import appears. No existing runtime file is modified. The Phase 3.21 patch does NOT introduce any new `GrowthEventType`, any new `GrowthEventSource`, any new `OperatorCommand`, any new `LOCAL_COMMAND_VERBS` entry, any new `ACTIVE_VIEWS` value, any new aggregate scalar field (no "developmental I-ness score", no "maturity score", no "milestone completion percent"), any new dispatcher kind, any new operator verb, any new persistence schema, any new autosave trigger, any new TLICA runtime mutation, any kernel surface change, any L1 / L2 cache semantic change, any parser change, any prompt change, any Pattern Ledger semantic change, any Coherence Monitor semantic change, any Growth Ledger semantic change, or any consciousness / sentience / subjective / semantic / truth / agency / self-modification / introspection / metacognition / desire / will / belief / understanding claim. The words "developmental", "milestone", and "trajectory" are used throughout in their **operational** sense (the runtime *develops a deterministic trajectory across the ten milestones*; the system *crosses a milestone* in the sequence) — never in any developmental-psychology or subjective sense. Every milestone is grounded in a human-development analogue at the level of **structural marker only**; ToyI has none of infancy, childhood, attention, preference, memory, learning, understanding, judgment, context, or vigilance in the psychological sense. `STREAM_APPEND` does not invoke `brain.tick.tick` or the LLM; the harness consumes zero real model calls regardless of `processing_window_size` or `feedback_mode`. The non-claim audit is the same `_FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS` tuple Phase 3.12c Coherence Monitor introduced; the new I-DEVMILE-11 static-audit fixture scans the harness module source and every `MODULE_PRODUCED_STRINGS` entry. `brain/.llm_cache/` remains gitignored. The TLICA Lean spec in `lean_reference/` is not contradicted: every new row is marked as Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3 source label), no Lean theorem is claimed, no existing REQUIRED row is modified.

> **Previous catalog version:** v0.25. Patches over v0.24 (Phase 3.15 L1 Cache Hygiene): +4 REQUIRED rows, +1 STRUCTURAL row, -1 DEFERRED row, OBSERVED unchanged, NOT-EXERCISED unchanged. Promotes `I-LLMCACHE-20` from `DEFERRED` to `REQUIRED` by binding a deterministic write-skip-at-cap admission policy with `L1_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES = 1024` to the existing `CachedClient` L1 transport cache at `brain/llm/client.py`. The L1 entry count never exceeds `L1_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES`; at cap, `CachedClient` does not write a new entry; existing entries remain present and readable; hits continue to read. The cache itself never evicts (bounded admission, not eviction). At-cap miss behavior is explicit: the inner client is still called and the response is still returned to the caller; only the cache write is skipped. Adds `I-LLMCACHE-23..26` covering at-cap miss inner-call discipline, observability (new `llm.cache_skip` event with payload exactly `{cache_key_prefix, reason}` and `reason="capacity"`; new `skip_count` counter on `CachedClient` alongside `hit_count` and `miss_count`), no-silent-repair guarantees (existing entries unchanged, corrupt entries still fail loud, no inner fall-back on corrupt read, no `llm.cache_skip` emission below cap), and a static AST audit (`I-LLMCACHE-26`) over `brain/llm/client.py` that rejects new forbidden imports and asserts the `llm.cache_skip` payload uses only `cache_key_prefix` and `reason`. L2 (`eval_v1`) semantics are unchanged: `SEMANTIC_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES = 1024`, `SEMANTIC_CACHE_DIR = brain/.llm_cache/eval_v1`, and `SEMANTIC_CACHE_SCHEMA_VERSION = "llm-semantic-cache-v1"` all remain. Offline remains the default; model-backed modes remain explicit opt-in; the Phase 3.14 flag contract (`--llm-disable-cache` wins over default-on; supplying both `--llm-enable-cache` and `--llm-disable-cache` raises `LlmRuntimeError`; OFFLINE / MOCK reject `--llm-enable-cache` at the factory boundary; `--llm-disable-cache` is a no-op for OFFLINE / MOCK) is preserved unchanged. `brain/tick.py` is not edited; `brain/development/growth_ledger.py`, `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py`, `brain/development/coherence_monitor.py`, persistence / autosave runtime files, scenarios, traces, `lean_reference/`, and `.claude/` are not edited; no `SCHEMA_VERSION` bump; no DB schema change; no UI expansion. `I-LLMCACHE-21` (real external model-backed cache smoke) and `I-LLMCACHE-22` (end-to-end Phase 3.14 behavior probe) remain `NOT-EXERCISED`; raw bad-response replay remains durable today (Option E deferred to a future campaign). No raw prompt / response / cache files committed; `brain/.llm_cache/` remains gitignored. "Bounded admission" is engineering language about cache write policy, not a claim about cognition.

> **Previous catalog version:** v0.24. Patches over v0.23 (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline catalog expansion): +18 REQUIRED rows, +1 STRUCTURAL row, +1 DEFERRED row, +2 NOT-EXERCISED rows; OBSERVED unchanged. Adds the `I-LLMCACHE-01..I-LLMCACHE-22` row family for a bounded, cataloged, observable LLM cache discipline that prevents repeated external model calls across ticks. L0 remains the per-instance `LLMBackedPtCns._cache` (unchanged). L1 is the existing prompt-hash transport cache (`CachedClient` at `brain/llm/client.py`); after a model-backed mode is explicitly selected, L1 is on by default and a new `--llm-disable-cache` opt-out flag forces it off; `--llm-enable-cache` remains accepted as an explicit affirmation; conflicting flags raise `LlmRuntimeError`. OFFLINE / MOCK still reject `--llm-enable-cache` and accept `--llm-disable-cache` as a no-op without unlocking cache access. L2 is a new canonical semantic evaluation cache implemented inside `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` (Option 3 per the Step 5 plan); its key is the SHA-256 hex of the deterministic `repr()` of the seven-tuple `(SEMANTIC_CACHE_SCHEMA_VERSION="llm-semantic-cache-v1", PROMPT_TEMPLATE_VERSION="prompt-template-v1", PARSE_SCHEMA_VERSION="consistency-eval-v1", backend_family, model_identity, existing_msi_context, new_text)` with `existing_msi_context` a sorted tuple of `(content_id, text)` pairs over non-cogito MSI contents; the evaluated `new_id` is intentionally excluded from the L2 key (LOCK E) but retained in the rendered prompt for diagnostics. L2 stores only parse-success entries with the exact JSON payload `{"key_prefix", "parsed"}` — raw prompt, raw response, error text, and provider metadata are never persisted to L2 files. The L2 directory is `brain/.llm_cache/eval_v1/`, covered by the existing gitignored `brain/.llm_cache/` root. L2 is capped at `SEMANTIC_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES = 1024`; at cap, hits still read, misses may call the explicit model-backed inner path but do not write a new entry and the implementation emits `llm.semantic_cache_skip` with `reason="capacity"`. Corrupt L1 / L2 entries fail loud with a bounded error and never silently call the inner client (`reason="parse_failure"` is emitted as a bounded skip event when retries exhaust without a parse-success). Failure classes (parse failure, provider failure, timeout, refusal / empty, schema mismatch, corrupt entry) are kept distinct and never collapse into one L2 cache state. Cache hit / miss / store / skip events are observable through the existing `CognitionTracer` interface as `llm.cache_hit`, `llm.cache_miss`, `llm.semantic_cache_hit`, `llm.semantic_cache_miss`, `llm.semantic_cache_store`, and `llm.semantic_cache_skip`; trace payloads carry only `content_id`, the 8-character `key_prefix`, and (where applicable) `reason` — never raw prompt or raw response. Dependency direction is one-way: `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` does not import `brain.ui.*` or `brain.tick`. The catalog patch keeps L1 unbounded (mark `I-LLMCACHE-20` DEFERRED) and registers real-external-LLM cache smoke (`I-LLMCACHE-21`) and end-to-end Phase 3.14 behavior probe (`I-LLMCACHE-22`) as NOT-EXERCISED in v1. The Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline does NOT modify `brain/tick.py`, `brain/development/growth_ledger.py`, `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py`, `brain/development/coherence_monitor.py`, `brain/ui/session.py`, persistence / autosave runtime files, scenarios, traces, `lean_reference/`, or `.claude/`; `(new_state, TickRecord)` parity at the kernel boundary is preserved bit-for-bit between cached and uncached evaluations for the same client responses. Offline remains the default; model-backed execution remains explicit opt-in; cache flags cannot promote OFFLINE / MOCK into a model-backed mode (mode selection remains governed by the existing `I-LLMTOG-*` family). "Semantic" in "semantic evaluation cache" is engineering language about cache identity, not a claim that ToyI understands meaning.

## Schema

| Column | Meaning |
|---|---|
| **ID** | Stable identifier `I-<MOD>-NN` for cross-referencing. |
| **Lean source** | `<file>::<decl>` — the authoritative theorem, definition, or structure field. |
| **Proposition** | Plain statement of what holds. |
| **Python assertion** | Pseudocode for the runtime check. |
| **Owning module** | The `brain/` file that hosts the assertion. |
| **Fixture** | The `brain/fixtures/` file that drives it. |
| **Status** | `REQUIRED` (must assert green in v0) · `STRUCTURAL` (type-enforced at construction or covered by another row's fixture; no per-tick assertion of its own) · `NOT-EXERCISED` (Python surface exists but no v0 fixture drives it) · `DEFERRED` (explicit non-goal per `CLAIM_GUARDRAILS.md` or Lean deferred marker) · `OBSERVED` (recorded in the run summary for inspection; does not fail the runner — used for properties useful to track but not required for correctness). |

## Conventions

- **Numeric core: `Fraction`.** All profile values, distances, ranks, and PCE values inside `brain/tlica/`, `brain/fixtures/`, and `brain/invariants.py` are `fractions.Fraction`. Type alias `Rho = Fraction`. Raw `==` is safe and used throughout the catalog. The constructor `rho(value: int | float | str | Fraction) -> Fraction` normalizes at the I/O boundary and raises if the value is outside `[0, 1]` — never silently clamps. `brain/io_types.PerceptEvent` accepts any of those input types; `TickRecord` may expose float views for display only, never for invariant checks.
- **`Act` is an `enum.Enum`**, not a `typing.Literal`:
  ```python
  class Act(str, Enum):
      NOOP = "noop"
      INTEGRATE = "integrate"
      DIFFERENTIATE = "differentiate"
      ENCAPSULATE = "encapsulate"
  ```
  `isinstance(x, Act)` works at runtime; `proj.no_action is Act.NOOP`.
- **Infinity.** `dInfShared` returns `math.inf` (a float, the single permitted float in the kernel) on empty intersection, matching Lean's `⊤`. All other distance/rank/PCE values are `Fraction`.
- **Distances.** `dInfUnion(f, g)` and `dInfShared(f, g)` are computed over `f.domain | g.domain` and `f.domain & g.domain` respectively — **not** the current content store's keys. Projected profiles have their own domains.
- **Cogito.** `COGITO_ID` is a reserved sentinel that cannot collide with user input. Cogito invariants (I-MSI-01, I-MSI-02, I-PTC-01) are enforced at construction via `brain/tlica/builders.py`, then re-asserted at every tick. v0 deterministic `ProjectMap` stubs are obligated to preserve `COGITO_ID` at value `1` in every projected profile (I-RT-07).
- **PCE vs ProjectedPCE.** Foundation `PCE` (`brain/tlica/pce.py`) is action-constant by Lean theorem (I-PCE-04). Action selection routes through `feasibleProjectedPCE` (`brain/tlica/agency.py` / `brain/tlica/action_projection.py`). The brain **never** uses foundation PCE for action choice (I-PCE-05).
- **Modes vs Actions.** `ModeOp` (A / B / C / neutral) and `Act` (NOOP / INTEGRATE / DIFFERENTIATE / ENCAPSULATE) are disjoint namespaces. Mode B is parallel, not triggered by `PtCns.fromEval`. The mapping from `ModeOp` to default `Act` is a lookup, not an identity.
- **`ProjectMap` exposes `natural_dynamics`.** Because Lean's `identity_action_natural` is an existential, the Python `ProjectMap` Protocol exposes `natural_dynamics(profile) -> ScalarProfile` explicitly so the witness is testable. v0 deterministic stub: `natural_dynamics(P) = P`.
- **Validation helpers live in `brain/validation.py`.** Reusable functions like `profile_equiv`, `is_in_unit_interval`, `assert_subset_rank_le` are owned by `brain/validation.py`, used by both `brain/invariants.py` and the fixtures. Constructors live in `brain/tlica/builders.py`. The catalog runner lives in `brain/invariants.py`. The dependency graph: `builders → validation`, `invariants → fixtures + validation`, `tick → builders + invariants`.

---

## Required v0 invariants

### `brain/tlica/profile.py` — `ScalarProfile`, `zeroExtend`

| ID | Lean source | Proposition | Python assertion | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|

| I-PROF-03 | `Profile.lean::zeroExtend_of_mem` | `zero_extend(x) == profile[x]` when `x ∈ domain`. | `profile.zero_extend(x) == profile.values[x]` for `x in profile.domain` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PROF-04 | `Profile.lean::zeroExtend_of_not_mem` | `zero_extend(x) == 0` when `x ∉ domain`. | `profile.zero_extend(x) == Fraction(0)` for `x not in profile.domain` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PROF-05 | `Profile.lean::zeroExtend_nonneg` | Zero-extension is non-negative everywhere. | `all(profile.zero_extend(x) >= 0 for x in universe)` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PROF-06 | `Profile.lean::zeroExtend_le_one` | Zero-extension is ≤ 1 everywhere. | `all(profile.zero_extend(x) <= 1 for x in universe)` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PROF-07 | `Profile.lean::abs_sub_zeroExtend_le_one` | Pointwise zero-extension difference is ≤ 1. | `all(abs(f.zero_extend(x) - g.zero_extend(x)) <= 1 for x in f.domain | g.domain)` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |

### `brain/tlica/preservation.py` — `PreservationRanking`

> **v0 stub signature (cogito-gated):**
> ```python
> def rank(S: frozenset[ContentID]) -> Fraction:
>     if COGITO_ID not in S:
>         return Fraction(0)
>     return Fraction(len(S & msi.contents), max(1, len(msi.contents)))
> ```
> This satisfies `rank_nonneg`, `cogito_necessity`, `no_cogito_zero_rank`, `msi_maximality`, and (by construction over the simple stub) `msi_monotonicity`.

| ID | Lean source | Proposition | Python assertion | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-PRES-01 | `PreservationRanking.lean::PreservationRanking.rank_nonneg` | Every set's rank is non-negative. | `all(pi.rank(S) >= 0 for S in test_sets)` | `minimal.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PRES-02 | `PreservationRanking.lean::PreservationRanking.cogito_necessity` (Axiom 4.3.1) | Rank > 0 implies cogito in set. | `for S in test_sets: pi.rank(S) > 0 ⇒ COGITO_ID in S` | `minimal.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PRES-03 | `PreservationRanking.lean::PreservationRanking.msi_maximality` (Axiom 4.3.2) | MSI realizes rank maximum. | `all(pi.rank(S) <= pi.rank(msi.contents) for S in test_sets)` | `minimal.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PRES-04 | `PreservationRanking.lean::no_cogito_zero_rank` | Sets without cogito have rank 0. | `pi.rank(S) == 0` when `COGITO_ID not in S` | `minimal.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PRES-05 | `PreservationRanking.lean::PreservationRanking.msi_monotonicity` (Axiom 4.3.3) | Conditional MSI-component monotonicity. | Holds by construction under the cogito-gated stub; covered by `minimal.py` sampling. | `minimal.py` | STRUCTURAL |

### `brain/tlica/project_map.py` — `ProjectMap`

> **Python Protocol exposes `natural_dynamics` explicitly:**
> ```python
> class ProjectMap(Protocol):
>     no_action: Act
>     def project(self, action: Act, profile: ScalarProfile) -> ScalarProfile: ...
>     def natural_dynamics(self, profile: ScalarProfile) -> ScalarProfile: ...
> ```
> v0 deterministic stub: `natural_dynamics(P) = P` (identity); `project(NOOP, P) = natural_dynamics(P)`.

| I-PMAP-02 | `ProjectMap.lean::ProjectMap.identity_action_natural` (Axiom 5.3.1) | `project(noAction, P)` equals natural dynamics. | `profile_equiv(proj.project(proj.no_action, P), proj.natural_dynamics(P))` | `trajectory_step.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PMAP-03 | `ProjectMap.lean::ProjectMap.noAction_projects` | `project(noAction, P)` is well-defined. | Total function — Python type system enforces. | — | STRUCTURAL |

### `brain/tlica/comparison/pointwise.py` — `dInfUnion`, `dInfShared`

> **Computable, finite-domain implementations:**
> ```python
> def d_inf_union(f, g):
>     vals = [abs(f.zero_extend(x) - g.zero_extend(x)) for x in f.domain | g.domain]
>     return max(vals) if vals else Fraction(0)
>
> def d_inf_shared(f, g):
>     shared = f.domain & g.domain
>     if not shared:
>         return math.inf
>     return max(abs(f.zero_extend(x) - g.zero_extend(x)) for x in shared)
> ```

| ID | Lean source | Proposition | Python assertion | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-PWS-01 | `Pointwise.lean::dInfUnion_nonneg` | `dInfUnion(f, g) ≥ 0`. | `d_inf_union(f, g) >= 0` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PWS-02 | `Pointwise.lean::dInfUnion_symm` | `dInfUnion(f, g) == dInfUnion(g, f)`. | `d_inf_union(f, g) == d_inf_union(g, f)` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PWS-03 | `Pointwise.lean::dInfUnion_self` | `dInfUnion(f, f) == 0`. | `d_inf_union(f, f) == 0` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PWS-04 | `Pointwise.lean::dInfUnion_le_one` | `dInfUnion(f, g) ≤ 1`. | `d_inf_union(f, g) <= 1` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PWS-05 | `Pointwise.lean::dInfUnion_triangle` | `dInfUnion(f, h) ≤ dInfUnion(f, g) + dInfUnion(g, h)`. | Triangle inequality across three test profiles. | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PWS-06 | `Pointwise.lean::dInfShared_nonneg` | `dInfShared(f, g) ≥ 0`. | `d_inf_shared(f, g) >= 0` (with `math.inf >= 0`) | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PWS-07 | `Pointwise.lean::dInfShared_symm` | `dInfShared(f, g) == dInfShared(g, f)`. | `d_inf_shared(f, g) == d_inf_shared(g, f)` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PWS-08 | `Pointwise.lean::dInfShared_self_of_nonempty` | Non-empty domain ⇒ `dInfShared(f, f) == 0`. | If `f.domain != set()`: `d_inf_shared(f, f) == 0` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PWS-09 | `Pointwise.lean::dInfShared_top_iff` | Empty intersection ⇔ `dInfShared(f, g) == ⊤`. | `d_inf_shared(f, g) == math.inf` iff `f.domain & g.domain == set()` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PWS-10 | `Pointwise.lean::dInfShared_le_one_of_nonempty` | Non-empty intersection ⇒ `dInfShared(f, g) ≤ 1`. | If shared non-empty: `d_inf_shared(f, g) <= 1` | `profile_distance.py` | REQUIRED |

| I-AFF-13 | `DifferentiatedAffect.lean::pceDefeating_not_neutral` | Defeating excludes neutral. | `pce_defeating(...) ⇒ not pce_neutral(...)` | `projected_pce.py` | REQUIRED |

### `brain/llm/` — LLM client seam (Phase 2 v1)

> The LLM-backed `PtCns.eval` layer. Foundation `PtCns` (the v0 dataclass) is unchanged; `LLMBackedPtCns` is a duck-typed alternative that consults an `LLMClient` Protocol.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-LLM-01 | Plan convention (Phase 2 v1) | `PtCns.eval` returns one of `{PRESERVE, DAMAGE, NEUTRAL}` after retry resolution. Up to 3 attempts; final failure raises and the tick fails. | `LLMBackedPtCns(content)` returns `ConsistencyEval` member; never returns sentinel "invalid"; raises `ValueError` on Nth-attempt failure. | `llm_protocol.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLM-02 | Plan convention (Phase 2 v1) | Cached identical prompts produce identical outputs. | Same prompt routed twice through `CachedClient` returns same response without re-calling the inner client. | `llm_protocol.py` | OBSERVED |
| I-LLM-03 | I-PTC-01 (cogito_invariance) | LLM-backed `PtCns.eval(COGITO_ID)` short-circuits to `PRESERVE` without an LLM call. | `LLMBackedPtCns.eval(COGITO_ID) == PRESERVE` and the underlying client is not called. | `llm_protocol.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLM-04 | Plan convention (Phase 2 v1) | The LLM-backed implementation honors the `LLMClient` Protocol — `eval_consistency(prompt: str) -> str`. No direct HTTP coupling, no provider lock-in. | `isinstance(client, LLMClient)` and `LLMBackedPtCns` accepts any conforming client. | `llm_protocol.py` | STRUCTURAL |

### `brain/trace.py` — Cognition trace seam (Phase 2 v1.1)

> The togglable observation seam: a `CognitionTracer` Protocol with three backends (`NullTracer`, `MemoryTracer`, `FileTracer`). The tracer is observation-only — `tick()` output must be byte-identical whether a tracer is present or not. Toggle via `BRAIN_TRACE_PATH` env var or `--trace` CLI flag; default is `NullTracer()`.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-TRACE-01 | Plan convention (Phase 2 v1.1) | The tracer is observation-only. `tick(state, events, client, tracer)` produces identical `(BrainState, TickRecord)` output regardless of which `CognitionTracer` backend is supplied. | Run the first scenario through each of `{NullTracer(), MemoryTracer(), FileTracer(tmp_path)}` with the same MockClient seed; assert all three final `BrainState` values are equal and all three `mode_trace` sequences are identical. | `trace_v1_1.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-TRACE-02 | Plan convention (Phase 2 v1.2 baseline hardening) | Tracer record failures do not propagate. `tick()` output is identical whether `tracer.record` raises or not. `SafeTracer` wraps every factory-built tracer and swallows backend exceptions. | Run the scenario through a `_TracerThatAlwaysRaises` wrapped in `SafeTracer`; assert resulting `BrainState` and `mode_trace` equal the `NullTracer` baseline. | `trace_v1_1.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-TRACE-03 | Plan convention (trace boundary hardening) | Tracer payloads cannot overwrite reserved event-envelope keys. `MemoryTracer` and `FileTracer` reject payloads containing `type`, `timestamp_ns`, or `tick_id`; `SafeTracer` preserves observation-only behavior by swallowing trace-sink validation failures. | Raw `MemoryTracer` and `FileTracer(tmp_path)` raise `ValueError` naming I-TRACE-03 on reserved keys; `SafeTracer(MemoryTracer())` and `SafeTracer(FileTracer(tmp_path))` swallow the same validation failure without recording an invalid event. | `trace_v1_1.py` | STRUCTURAL |

### Behavioral (Phase 2 v1)

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-BHV-01 | Plan convention (Phase 2 v1, criterion 3) | Given a forced eval sequence (via MockClient seeded from `expected_eval`), the resulting mode trace matches `expected_mode`. Verifies the eval→mode→state-update orchestration; *does not* verify LLM behavior. | After running `scenarios/first_scenario_v1.json`: `actual_modes == [tick["expected_mode"] for tick in scenario.ticks]`. | `scenario_v1.py` | REQUIRED |

> **Note.** I-BHV-01 verifies the brain's deterministic orchestration of eval→mode under controlled MockClient inputs. The actual LLM behavioral check (does the LLM correctly classify the scenario's percepts?) happens in `python -m brain.scenario run …` with a real `AnthropicAPIClient` and is not part of the runner gate.

## Modules with no v0-required invariants

### `brain/tlica/mode_aggregation.py`, `brain/tlica/dynamics.py`

These cover Proposition 2.5.1 (convergence of the mode-aggregation series) and Proposition 5.7.2 (uniform convergence by M-test). Both reason about genuinely infinite sums; v0 commits to finite-at-each-tick (summation over finite content store). Python equivalents may expose a truncated `finite_mode_aggregation(...)` for fixture use, but no invariant in v0 depends on convergence. Status: **NOT-EXERCISED** in v0; thin module with docstring + truncated computation.

### `brain/tlica/non_reducibility.py`

Covers Theorem 6.5.1 (formal non-reducibility). Requires the non-Archimedean δ that v0 drops. Status: **DEFERRED** in v0; docstring-only.

### `brain/tlica/comparison/shell_refinement.py`, `brain/tlica/comparison/pseudo_emetric.py`

Shell-stratified distance bounds and pseudo-emetric instance. v0 exposes the types so the public surface matches the Lean, but no fixture drives them. Status: **NOT-EXERCISED**.

---

## Cross-cutting / runtime-only invariants

These are not Lean theorems but are needed for the runtime to be coherent. Owned by `brain/invariants.py`, `brain/tlica/builders.py`, and `brain/tick.py`.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-RT-01 | Plan convention | `COGITO_ID` does not appear in any user-supplied `PerceptEvent`. | At ingest: `event.content_id != COGITO_ID` raises. | `brain/io_types.py` |
| I-RT-02 | Plan convention | Profile values stay in `[0, 1]` across every tick transition. | After each mode operator: re-assert I-PROF-01 and I-PROF-02. | `brain/tick.py` |
| I-RT-03 | Plan convention | MSI density is maintained across transitions. | After each mode operator: re-assert I-MSI-03. | `brain/tick.py` |
| I-RT-04 | Plan convention | PtCns evaluations remain a total function over the current profile domain. | After each tick: assert `set(ptcns.eval_map.keys()) == set(profile.domain)`. | `brain/tick.py` |
| I-RT-05 | Plan convention | The tick log is append-only; no state is mutated retroactively. | `TickRecord` instances are frozen dataclasses. | `brain/io_types.py` |
| I-RT-06 | Plan convention | Builders fail loudly on invalid construction (no silent clamping; out-of-bounds values raise). | `make_profile_with_cogito`, `make_msi`, `make_ptcns` raise `ValueError` on violation. | `brain/tlica/builders.py` |
| I-RT-07 | Plan convention | Every projected profile produced by v0 `ProjectMap` preserves `COGITO_ID` at value `1`. | After every `project(a, P)`: `COGITO_ID in projected.domain and projected.values[COGITO_ID] == 1`. | `brain/tlica/project_map.py` + `brain/tick.py` |

The kernel never sees an invalid state mid-trajectory. | After each `tick(state, events, client)` call, `brain/tick.py::assert_state_invariants(new_state)` re-asserts the runtime-applicable v0.2 rows; the scenario fixture asserts no exception escapes the loop. | `brain/tick.py` | `scenario_v1.py` | REQUIRED |
