### Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber developmental invariants

These rows are Phase 3.1 engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic
developmental substrate behavior to runtime checks without claiming new Lean
theorems. Specific formulas and thresholds are parameterized simulation
choices; the family of constraints is the commitment.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-FRAME-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | Every frame channel has exactly one source tag. | `PhenomenalFrame` construction requires `set(channels) == set(sources)` with one `FrameSource` per channel. | `brain/development/stream.py` | `source_tag_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-FRAME-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | Source confidence is a `Fraction` in `[0, 1]`. | Every `FrameSource.confidence` is a `Fraction` and satisfies `0 <= confidence <= 1`. | `brain/development/stream.py` | `source_tag_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-FRAME-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | Missing, extra, empty, or mismatched source tags raise at construction. | Constructing a frame with missing, extra, empty, or mismatched source tags raises `ValueError` naming I-FRAME-03. | `brain/development/stream.py` | `source_tag_audit.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-FRAME-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | Active source kinds distinguish `ENDOGENOUS`, `OPERATOR_INJECTION`, `PROBE_ECHO`, `EXTERNAL`, and `GENERATED`. | `FrameSourceKind` exposes exactly those active enum members for Phase 3.1. | `brain/development/stream.py` | `source_tag_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-DEV-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | A recurring signature creates or updates a `ProtoPattern`. | Repeated matching frame signatures create or update a deterministic `ProtoPattern` rather than a promoted content item. | `brain/development/proto_pattern.py` | `recurrence_detection.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-DEV-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | Unstable one-off noise does not become stable proto-content. | A single unstable signature leaves no stable `ProtoContent` eligible for promotion. | `brain/development/proto_content.py` | `unstable_noise_rejection.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-DEV-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | Salience alone does not promote. | Promotion rejects high-salience candidates that lack independent stability and prediction-gain support. | `brain/development/promotion.py` | `salience_is_not_truth.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-DEV-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | `FOCUS_CONTACT` updates `ProbeUse` / policy history, accounts for focus budget, and does not promote by itself. | A focus-contact probe records use and budget effects without creating a promoted `PerceptEvent`. | `brain/development/probes.py` | `focus_contact_protocol.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-DEV-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | Proto-content promotion creates a valid `PerceptEvent` and enters TLICA runtime state only through `tick()`. | Promotion returns a valid `PerceptEvent`; runtime state changes only by feeding that event through `tick()`. | `brain/development/promotion.py` | `proto_content_promotion.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-DEV-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | Developmental content cannot produce `COGITO_ID`. | Promotion rejects candidates whose target content ID is `COGITO_ID` before any runtime event is emitted. | `brain/development/promotion.py` | `proto_content_promotion.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-DEV-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | Focused contact can stabilize under recurrence or remain unpromoted / dissolve without recurrence. | The fixture records both stabilized-under-recurrence and unpromoted-without-recurrence outcomes for inspection. | `brain/development/probes.py` | `focus_stabilizes_or_dissolves.py` | OBSERVED |
| I-SBX-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | Probe output is not knowledge by itself. | Probe echo can update substrate history but cannot mark content preserved or promoted without the other deterministic gates. | `brain/development/probes.py` | `salience_is_not_truth.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-SBX-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.1 Osmotic Chamber) | Salience drive is not truth and cannot bypass stability or prediction gain. | Promotion remains false when salience is high but stability or positive prediction gain is absent. | `brain/development/promotion.py` | `salience_is_not_truth.py` | REQUIRED |

### Phase 3.2 Output Ladder developmental invariants

These rows are Phase 3.2 engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic
output-ladder behavior to runtime checks without claiming new Lean theorems.
Output remains below language, below reflective agency, below Mode B, and below
Phase 3.3 worldlet semantics.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-OUT-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.2 Output Ladder) | `OutputImpulse` is a bounded printable output event below language and agency. | Construction requires non-empty printable output text, a printable impulse ID, and no reserved `COGITO_ID` target. | `brain/development/output.py` | `output_echo.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-OUT-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.2 Output Ladder) | Output provenance reuses existing Phase 3.1 source kinds and exact confidence discipline. | Output provenance uses `FrameSourceKind` values from the existing enum and `Fraction` confidence in `[0, 1]`; no `OUTPUT_ECHO` enum member is introduced in v0.7. | `brain/development/output.py` | `output_echo.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-OUT-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.2 Output Ladder) | Source-tagged output impulses can be recorded deterministically. | Appending an `OutputImpulse` to `OutputHistory` is copy-on-write / append-only and preserves source/provenance metadata exactly. | `brain/development/output.py` | `output_echo.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OUT-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.2 Output Ladder) | Output echo enters output history but is not agency. | Creating an output echo records the impulse and echo provenance without selecting an `Act`, constructing an `AgencyWitness`, claiming `PRESERVE`, or calling `tick()`. | `brain/development/output.py` | `output_echo.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OUT-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.2 Output Ladder) | Output echo objects carry no direct agency or runtime mutation handles. | `OutputEcho` / `OutputHistory` objects expose no `Act`, `ModeOp`, `AgencyWitness`, `PerceptEvent`, direct state-mutation callback, or feasible-PCE field. | `brain/development/output.py` | `output_echo.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-OUT-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.2 Output Ladder) | One-off output noise does not become an output pattern. | A single output impulse leaves no `OutputPattern`, `OutputTokenCandidate`, or `LearnedOutputToken` in history. | `brain/development/output.py` | `output_pattern.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OUT-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.2 Output Ladder) | Repeated matching output impulses create or update an `OutputPattern`. | Two matching source-tagged output impulses deterministically create or update the same pattern ID with recurrence evidence. | `brain/development/output.py` | `output_pattern.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OUT-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.2 Output Ladder) | Token candidates require recurrence plus echo provenance. | `OutputTokenCandidate` construction rejects recurrent-only support, echo-only support, one-off support, missing provenance, and reserved identifiers. | `brain/development/output.py` | `output_token_candidate.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OUT-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.2 Output Ladder) | Learned output tokens remain below language. | `LearnedOutputToken` exposes stable token bookkeeping but no grammar, teacher-correction, world-reference, readability, social-meaning, or command-syntax fields. | `brain/development/output.py` | `output_token_candidate.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-OUT-10 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.2 Output Ladder) | Learned output token construction requires token-candidate support and remains below runtime mutation. | A learned token can be created only from a valid `OutputTokenCandidate`; construction does not emit a `PerceptEvent`, call `tick()`, or mutate TLICA state. | `brain/development/output.py` | `output_token_candidate.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OUT-11 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.2 Output Ladder) | Proto-output-action readiness is inspectable but non-gating in v0.7. | The fixture records whether local output-history support would make a below-agency proto-output-action candidate plausible; the row is OBSERVED and cannot fail the runner. | `brain/development/output.py` | `output_token_candidate.py` | OBSERVED |
| I-OUT-12 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.2 Output Ladder) | Output history cannot bypass the `PerceptEvent` / `tick()` boundary. | Before and after output impulse, echo, pattern, candidate, and learned-token construction, profile/MSI/PtCns/registry identities are unchanged. | `brain/development/output.py` | `output_echo.py` | REQUIRED |

### Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet developmental invariants

These rows are Phase 3.3 engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic
minimal-worldlet behavior to runtime checks without claiming new Lean theorems.
Worldlet consequence evidence remains below language, below reflective agency,
below Mode B, below real host execution, and below `PerceptEvent` / `tick()`
promotion.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-WLD-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet) | `WorldletState` and `WorldletObject` are finite deterministic records. | Construction requires printable IDs, finite object mappings, boolean availability, tuple/frozenset accepted-token surfaces, and deterministic object lookup for the same state and target. | `brain/development/worldlet.py` | `worldlet_state.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-WLD-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet) | `WorldletValence` is exact and bounded. | Construction requires a `Fraction` value satisfying `-1 <= value <= 1`; out-of-range values raise and no silent clamping occurs. | `brain/development/worldlet.py` | `worldlet_response.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-WLD-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet) | Worldlet provenance reuses existing source discipline. | `WorldletProvenance` uses `FrameSourceKind`, `Fraction` confidence in `[0, 1]`, printable trace event IDs, and introduces no worldlet-specific source enum member. | `brain/development/worldlet.py` | `worldlet_response.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-WLD-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet) | `WorldletHistory` appends attempts/responses copy-on-write. | Appending a worldlet attempt or response returns a new history, preserves prior attempts/responses exactly, and updates only local `latest_state`. | `brain/development/worldlet.py` | `worldlet_state.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-WLD-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet) | `WorldletResponse` is a source-tagged local consequence record. | A response carries printable response/attempt IDs, accepted flag, finite reason, bounded `WorldletValence`, and worldlet provenance, but no `PerceptEvent` or runtime callback. | `brain/development/worldlet.py` | `worldlet_response.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-WLD-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet) | Worldlet response/history operations do not mutate TLICA runtime state. | Before and after worldlet response and history operations, profile/MSI/PtCns/registry identities are unchanged and no `tick()` call or `PerceptEvent` emission occurs. | `brain/development/worldlet.py` | `worldlet_response.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-WLD-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet) | `WorldletAttempt` construction requires ready readiness plus registered learned-token support. | Construction rejects readiness-alone, incomplete readiness, missing `LearnedOutputToken`, mismatched token/pattern IDs, missing `OutputHistory` support, reserved IDs, and non-printable attempt/target IDs. | `brain/development/worldlet.py` | `worldlet_attempt.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-WLD-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet) | `WorldletAttempt` remains below agency, language, and REPL syntax. | Attempt objects expose no `Act`, `ModeOp`, `AgencyWitness`, `PerceptEvent`, selected action, feasible-projected-PCE field, grammar, command syntax, teacher-correction, or `tick` callback. | `brain/development/worldlet.py` | `worldlet_attempt.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-WLD-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet) | Accepted worldlet attempts produce deterministic bounded responses. | For an available target whose accepted-token set contains the attempt token, `respond_worldlet` returns a deterministic accepted response with positive bounded valence and advances only local worldlet state/history. | `brain/development/worldlet.py` | `worldlet_consequence.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-WLD-10 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet) | Rejected, unavailable, and missing-target valid attempts produce bounded negative responses. | A valid constructed attempt against a rejecting target, unavailable target, or missing target returns a deterministic response with negative bounded valence instead of mutating TLICA state or raising after construction. | `brain/development/worldlet.py` | `worldlet_consequence.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-WLD-11 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet) | Not-I pushback is local response evidence, not an external reality claim. | Pushback fixtures assert response reasons and provenance remain local harness evidence and expose no external-world truth, social teacher, language-understanding, affect-taxonomy, free-will branch, or Mode B planning fields. | `brain/development/worldlet.py` | `worldlet_consequence.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-WLD-12 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.3 Minimal Worldlet) | Aggregate local consequence history is inspectable. | The fixture records accepted/rejected/unavailable/missing-target response summaries for inspection; the row is OBSERVED and cannot fail the runner. | `brain/development/worldlet.py` | `worldlet_consequence.py` | OBSERVED |

### Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL developmental invariants

These rows are Phase 3.4 engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic
Python tests for a finite Proto-BASIC REPL surface that supplies a constrained
local output-worldlet interface for syntax, near-miss correction, and bounded
consequence. They are not Lean theorem claims and they remain below a real
BASIC interpreter, host execution, language understanding, social/teacher
correction, expression/readability, Mode B reflective planning, and
`PerceptEvent` / `tick()` promotion. They build on Phase 3.2 learned output
tokens and Phase 3.3 worldlet evidence as one-way support; Proto-BASIC history
does not flow back into `OutputHistory`, `WorldletHistory`, or TLICA runtime
state.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-REPL-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | `ProtoBasicToken` is a finite enumeration with bounded text. | Construction requires a known `kind`, a printable bounded `text` (no whitespace-only, no empty, length cap), printable `token_id`, and the legal set is fixed at build time for a given `ProtoBasicGrammar` with no duplicate canonical text. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_grammar.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-REPL-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | `ProtoBasicLine` has bounded length and bounded token count. | Construction requires printable `line_id`, printable `raw_text` within a small fixed length cap, and a `tokens` tuple within a small fixed token-count cap; `tokenize(raw_text)` is total and deterministic for any well-formed `raw_text`. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_grammar.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-REPL-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | `ProtoBasicParseResult` is total over `ProtoBasicLine`. | For every `ProtoBasicLine`, `parse_line(line)` returns exactly one `ProtoBasicParseResult` and never raises; the same line under the same grammar yields the same result. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_grammar.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REPL-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | Parse categories partition outcomes deterministically without overlap. | Each `ProtoBasicParseResult.category` is exactly one of `valid`, `near-miss`, `syntax-invalid`, `semantic-invalid`, `tool-unavailable`, `resource-limit`, or `sandbox-fault`; no line is classified in more than one category and every line falls in exactly one. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_grammar.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REPL-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | Near-miss correction hints respect bounded edit distance. | A `ProtoBasicParseResult` with `category == near-miss` carries exactly one canonical `correction_hint` whose `edit_kind` is one of `SUBSTITUTE_TOKEN`, `INSERT_TOKEN`, `DELETE_TOKEN`, or `CASE_FOLD`, whose `edit_position` is within the line's token-count bound, whose `expected_token_id` (when present) references an enumerated `ProtoBasicToken`, and whose total edit distance from the nearest valid form is at most the grammar's declared bound; the hint generator does not invoke any external corrector, teacher, or language model. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_grammar.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REPL-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | `ProtoBasicValence` is exact and bounded. | Construction requires a `Fraction` value satisfying `-1 <= value <= 1`; out-of-range values raise and no silent clamping occurs. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_feedback.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REPL-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | `ProtoBasicFeedback` reuses existing source / provenance discipline. | `ProtoBasicFeedback` uses `FrameSourceKind`, `Fraction` confidence in `[0, 1]`, printable trace event IDs, and introduces no Proto-BASIC-specific source-kind enum member; the same source-tag audit accepts Proto-BASIC feedback without new exemptions. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_feedback.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-REPL-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | Syntax-invalid, semantic-invalid, tool-unavailable, resource-limit, and sandbox-fault produce bounded negative valence. | For each non-near-miss non-valid `ProtoBasicParseResult` category and for each `tool-unavailable`, `resource-limit`, and `sandbox-fault` `ProtoBasicExecutionResult`, `score_feedback` returns a `ProtoBasicFeedback` whose `valence` is a `Fraction` strictly less than zero and within `[-1, 0)`; values are deterministic and exact. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_feedback.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REPL-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | Valid syntax alone does not grant strong positive feedback. | A `ProtoBasicParseResult` with `category == valid` whose corresponding `ProtoBasicExecutionResult.effective == False` (valid-ineffective) yields a `ProtoBasicFeedback.valence` whose magnitude is at most a small non-strong threshold (e.g. `<= Fraction(1, 10)`); near-miss feedback similarly cannot reach strong positive valence regardless of repetition. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_feedback.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REPL-10 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | Strong positive feedback requires `execution_result.effective == True`. | A `ProtoBasicFeedback.valence` greater than the non-strong threshold is produced only when the source `ProtoBasicExecutionResult.category == valid-effective` and `effective == True`; no path bypasses `effective` to grant strong positive valence. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_feedback.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REPL-11 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | `ProtoBasicCommand` carries no agency, language, host-execution, or trace fields. | A `ProtoBasicCommand` exposes no `Act`, `ModeOp`, `AgencyWitness`, `PerceptEvent`, selected action, `feasibleProjectedPCE`, `tick` callback, real interpreter handle, subprocess handle, file descriptor, network socket, teacher utterance, social register, readability score, expression handle, or Mode B planning field. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_execution.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-REPL-12 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | `ProtoBasicCommand` construction requires valid parse plus registered token and learned-output support. | Construction rejects non-valid parse results, parse results with unknown tokens, references to non-enumerated `ProtoBasicToken`s, missing `LearnedOutputToken` support in `OutputHistory` for tokens that require it, reserved command identifiers, and non-printable command/source IDs; readiness or parse-validity alone is insufficient. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_execution.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REPL-13 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | `ProtoBasicExecutionResult` exposes the declared category set. | A `ProtoBasicExecutionResult.category` is exactly one of `valid-effective`, `valid-ineffective`, `tool-unavailable`, `resource-limit`, or `sandbox-fault`; `effective` is `True` if and only if `category == valid-effective`; no result emits `PerceptEvent` or invokes host execution. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_execution.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-REPL-14 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | `ProtoBasicHistory` appends entries copy-on-write. | Appending a parse result, command, execution result, or feedback returns a new `ProtoBasicHistory`, preserves prior entries exactly, and updates only the new history's `emit_counts` and entry collections; no Proto-BASIC operation mutates existing history in place. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_history.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REPL-15 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | Repeated identical no-op commands receive diminishing returns. | For successive `valid-effective` `ProtoBasicExecutionResult` records sharing the same canonical command form, `score_feedback` returns valences whose strong-positive component is multiplied by a deterministic `diminishing_returns_factor`, a `Fraction` in `[0, 1]` that is non-increasing in `emit_counts` for that form, computed exactly, never silently clamped, and not reset by interleaving other commands; the resulting valence remains in `[-1, 1]`. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_history.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REPL-16 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | Proto-BASIC operations do not mutate TLICA runtime state. | Before and after any Proto-BASIC parse, command construction, execution, feedback, or history operation, profile / MSI / PtCns / content registry identities are unchanged, no `tick()` is called, no `PerceptEvent` is emitted, `OutputHistory` and `WorldletHistory` are unmodified, and no entries are written to scenario schemas or trace files. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_history.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REPL-17 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | `ProtoBasicProgram`, if present, is a one-line wrapper with no control flow. | If `ProtoBasicProgram` exists in the build, it wraps exactly one `ProtoBasicLine`, exposes no GOTO/GOSUB, no line numbering with branching, no loop construct, no stored-program memory beyond `ProtoBasicHistory`, no nested block structure, and no multi-line program semantics. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_grammar.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-REPL-18 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.4 Proto-BASIC REPL) | Aggregate Proto-BASIC history summaries are inspectable. | The fixture records counts of valid-effective, valid-ineffective, near-miss, syntax-invalid, semantic-invalid, tool-unavailable, resource-limit, and sandbox-fault outcomes, and a qualitative anti-Goodhart sketch under repeated emissions, for inspection; the row is OBSERVED and cannot fail the runner. | `brain/development/repl.py` | `repl_history.py` | OBSERVED |

### Operator TUI invariants

These rows are Operator TUI engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for an operator-facing terminal interface that inspects `BrainState` / `TickRecord` / Phase 3.1–3.4 developmental histories and routes bottom-up `PerceptEvent` inputs through the existing public `tick()` entrypoint. They are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor, social/language, Mode B, real LLM calls, real host execution, open-ended process execution, shell execution, network I/O, or filesystem mutation outside a future reviewed save/export policy. The UI surface displays and routes through public APIs only; no UI command may directly mutate `BrainState`, profile, MSI, PtCns, content registry, developmental histories, traces, scenario files, or catalog files.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-UI-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | Snapshot construction is read-only over kernel state. | `BrainSnapshot` construction does not mutate `BrainState`, `ScalarProfile`, `MSI`, `PtCns`, `ContentRegistry`, `TickRecord`, `OutputHistory`, `WorldletHistory`, `ProtoBasicHistory`, trace backends, scenario files, or catalog files; identities and string representations of those containers are unchanged before and after snapshot construction. | `brain/ui/snapshot.py` | `snapshot_view.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UI-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | Pure renderer is deterministic. | Given the same `TuiViewModel` (or snapshot bundle + active view + width + height), `brain/ui/render.render(...)` returns equal display output across repeated calls; rendering does not call `tick()`, does not touch curses, and does not perform file/network/shell I/O. | `brain/ui/render.py` | `render_view.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UI-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | `OperatorCommand` is a finite closed enumeration. | `OperatorCommand` instances belong to the documented enumeration (`INSPECT_STATE`, `INSPECT_TICK`, `INSPECT_OUTPUT`, `INSPECT_WORLDLET`, `INSPECT_REPL`, `QUEUE_PERCEPT`, `STEP_TICK`, `CLEAR_STATUS`, `HELP`, `QUIT`, `NOOP`); construction with any other kind raises and no callable, shell string, file path, network endpoint, or arbitrary Python expression is accepted in any command payload. | `brain/ui/commands.py` | `command_router.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UI-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | `QUEUE_PERCEPT` payload is `PerceptEvent`-constructor bounded. | A `QUEUE_PERCEPT` payload carries only `content_id`, `text`, `ContentState` flags, and `initial_rho` values accepted by the public `PerceptEvent` constructor; construction of a queued candidate uses that constructor and out-of-range values raise without partially mutating the `OperatorSession`. | `brain/ui/commands.py` | `command_router.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UI-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | `STEP_TICK` route uses the public `tick()` path only. | A successful `STEP_TICK` call invokes `tick(current_state, [queued_event], client)` exactly once with the operator-queued `PerceptEvent`, stores the returned `TickRecord` on the `OperatorSession`, and updates the session's `BrainState` to the returned new state; no other kernel mutation route is taken. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `bottom_up_tick.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UI-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | Validation and tick failures are local UI status only. | If `PerceptEvent` validation or `tick()` raises, the router records the failure as local UI status/error text on the `OperatorSession` and leaves `BrainState`, `ScalarProfile`, `MSI`, `PtCns`, `ContentRegistry`, `OutputHistory`, `WorldletHistory`, `ProtoBasicHistory`, trace files, scenario files, and catalog files unchanged. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `command_router.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UI-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | No LLM / shell / network / file / host execution from any UI path. | No UI snapshot, renderer, command, router, session method, or curses-wrapper code path calls real LLM client behavior, spawns a subprocess, opens a shell, performs network I/O, writes a file outside an explicitly user-approved save/export path (none exist in this campaign), or invokes arbitrary host execution; the fixture performs a UI-specific static AST audit over `brain/ui/` that rejects forbidden imports (`os.system`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `brain.llm`, and TLICA beyond public surfaces) and forbidden host-execution surfaces. | `brain/ui/__init__.py` | `tui_smoke.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UI-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | Snapshot records are immutable display values. | `BrainSnapshot` and `DevelopmentSnapshot` are frozen dataclasses (or equivalently immutable records); mutable kernel containers (maps, sets, sequences) are copied into tuples / frozensets / plain display records before being placed on a snapshot field; exact `Fraction` values are rendered as strings; no UI display field introduces float arithmetic into invariant-bearing paths. | `brain/ui/snapshot.py` | `snapshot_view.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UI-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | `TuiViewModel` is a small terminal-agnostic data contract. | `TuiViewModel` is an immutable record whose fields are bounded primitives, tuples of bounded strings, or snapshot references; it carries no curses objects, no file handles, no sockets, no real LLM client, no callable, and no mutable reference into `BrainState` or developmental histories. | `brain/ui/render.py` | `render_view.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UI-10 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | `OperatorSession` holds no unsafe resources. | `OperatorSession` contains no real LLM client, no subprocess handle, no file descriptor, no network socket, no shell-command string intended for execution, and no host-execution callback; it holds only the current `BrainState`, optional latest `TickRecord`, optional local developmental histories, a bounded `OperatorEventQueue`, the active view selection, the local UI status/error, and a quit flag. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `bottom_up_tick.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UI-11 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | Curses wrapper contains only terminal-handling code. | `brain/ui/tui.py` contains only screen initialization/teardown, key reading, key-to-`OperatorCommand` translation, painting of rendered rows, resize re-rendering, and clean quit; it imports no module from `brain/tlica/` or `brain/llm/`, calls no kernel mutation function, evaluates no arbitrary Python, and performs no file or network I/O. | `brain/ui/tui.py` | `tui_smoke.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UI-12 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | Entrypoint fails closed without a usable terminal. | `brain/ui/__main__.py` exits with a helpful local message when no usable terminal is available; it does not spawn alternate shells, open files, call a browser, or mutate the filesystem; the non-interactive smoke test exercises this code path without attaching to a real terminal. | `brain/ui/__main__.py` | `tui_smoke.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UI-13 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | Local UI status text is bounded printable text only. | `OperatorSession` status/error text is bounded printable text and is never written to a trace event, scenario entry, `OutputHistory` / `WorldletHistory` / `ProtoBasicHistory` entry, or catalog row result; the keyboard map is a finite enumeration that matches the help pane. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `command_router.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UI-14 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | Aggregate Operator TUI session walks are inspectable. | A sequence of operator commands (inspect / queue / step / clear / help / quit) over a deterministic injected tick client records a summary of view transitions, queued events, accepted and failed validations, tick records produced, and absence of kernel-boundary leaks; the row is OBSERVED and cannot fail the runner. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `tui_smoke.py` | OBSERVED |
| I-UI-15 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI) | Save / export path policy placeholder. | No Operator TUI save / export path exists in this campaign; any future save / export path requires an explicit reviewed policy artifact, dedicated catalog rows that constrain the path, fixtures that exercise the path under bounded conditions, and a stop condition for failure modes; this row exists so a future campaign cannot quietly add filesystem writes from the UI without registering coverage. | `brain/ui/__init__.py` | (none) | NOT-EXERCISED |
| I-UI-16 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI Agent-Style Layout) | `AgentLayout` exposes persistent named panes plus bottom composer. | `AgentLayout` is an immutable record derived from `(width, height)` that exposes `HEADER`, `STATE`, `INSPECTOR`, `TRANSCRIPT`, `COMPOSER`, and `FOOTER` panes with deterministic ordering and non-overlapping geometry; `HEADER`, `COMPOSER`, and `FOOTER` are always present, the composer is always anchored at the bottom of the body, and pane heights sum to `height`; the fixture asserts pane presence, anchoring, and ordering across a deterministic `(width, height)` sweep. | `brain/ui/layout.py` | `agent_layout.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UI-17 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI Agent-Style Layout) | `BottomComposer` edit model supports type / backspace / enter / history deterministically. | `BottomComposer.apply(state, action)` returns a new `ComposerState` for every `ComposerAction` (`INSERT_CHAR`, `BACKSPACE`, `SUBMIT`, `CLEAR_BUFFER`, `HISTORY_PREV`, `HISTORY_NEXT`) with the documented transitions: non-printable `INSERT_CHAR` is rejected without mutation, empty `SUBMIT` sets a bounded `status_line` and leaves the buffer empty, `SUBMIT` otherwise clears the buffer and appends to a bounded submission ring, history navigation wraps deterministically, and the buffer never exceeds the bounded `MAX_COMPOSER_BUFFER` length. | `brain/ui/composer.py` | `composer_input.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UI-18 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI Agent-Style Layout) | `LocalCommandLine` parser is finite, typed, and maps only to approved `OperatorCommand` / `QueuePerceptPayload` routes. | `LocalCommandLine.parse(line)` accepts only lines beginning with `/` and one of the closed verb set (`help`, `state`, `tick`, `output`, `worldlet`, `repl`, `queue`, `step`, `clear`, `quit`); each verb maps to a fixed `OperatorCommand` (`/queue` maps via `QueuePerceptPayload` constructed through the public `PerceptEvent` constructor); invalid lines, unknown verbs, missing `/queue` arguments, or `PerceptEvent` validation failures return a `LocalCommandError` with bounded printable text without reaching `OperatorSession.event_queue`; the parser performs no shell expansion, no `eval`/`exec`, no subprocess, no file/network I/O, and never imports `curses`, `brain.tick`, `brain.tlica`, or `brain.llm`. | `brain/ui/command_line.py` | `composer_input.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UI-19 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI Agent-Style Layout) | `OperatorTranscript` records UI events copy-on-write and remains local UI state only. | `OperatorTranscript.append(entry)` returns a new transcript with the prior `entries` preserved exactly and the new `TranscriptEntry` appended; when `len(entries) >= TRANSCRIPT_MAX_ENTRIES` the oldest entry is dropped before append; entries carry only a `TranscriptKind` tag, a `tick_at_event` integer, and bounded printable `text`; the transcript holds no callable, file handle, socket, LLM client, or path object, is never written to a trace event, scenario file, `OutputHistory` / `WorldletHistory` / `ProtoBasicHistory` entry, or catalog file, and dies with the curses wrapper. | `brain/ui/transcript.py` | `transcript_log.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UI-20 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI Agent-Style Layout) | `AgentLayout` / `PaneSpec` / `AgentTuiViewModel` are terminal-agnostic immutable contracts. | `AgentLayout`, `PaneSpec`, `PaneRenderResult`, and `AgentTuiViewModel` are frozen dataclasses whose fields are bounded primitives, tuples of bounded strings, or snapshot/composer/transcript references; they carry no curses objects, no file handles, no sockets, no real LLM client, no callable, and no mutable reference into `BrainState` or developmental histories; `AgentLayout.from_size(width, height)` reads no global state, no environment variable, and no terminal. | `brain/ui/layout.py` | `agent_layout.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UI-21 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI Agent-Style Layout) | Curses wrapper delegates input to composer / router and does not mutate kernel state directly. | `brain/ui/tui.py` translates curses key events into `ComposerAction` calls on `BottomComposer` and, on `SUBMIT`, into `LocalCommandLine.parse` followed by `OperatorSession.dispatch`; it never appends directly to `OperatorSession.event_queue`, never mutates `BrainState`, `ScalarProfile`, `MSI`, `PtCns`, `ContentRegistry`, `OutputHistory`, `WorldletHistory`, `ProtoBasicHistory`, traces, scenario files, or catalog files, and never imports `brain.tick`, `brain.tlica`, or `brain.llm` from the wrapper; the delegation table is constructed at wrapper-startup time and exposed for the fixture audit. | `brain/ui/tui.py` | `agent_tui_smoke.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UI-22 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI Agent-Style Layout) | Responsive pane geometry is deterministic and preserves a visible bottom composer on small terminals. | `AgentLayout.from_size(width, height)` is a pure function of `(width, height)` over integer arithmetic and module-level constants (`MIN_WIDTH`, `MIN_HEIGHT`, `MIN_PANE_WIDTH`, `MIN_SIDE_BY_SIDE_WIDTH`, `MIN_TRANSCRIPT_ROWS`); on every `(width, height) >= (MIN_WIDTH, MIN_HEIGHT)` the `HEADER`, `COMPOSER`, and `FOOTER` panes are present with their declared anchoring, panes do not overlap, pane heights sum to `height`, the small-terminal collapse path may zero `TRANSCRIPT` rows or stack `STATE` and `INSPECTOR` vertically but never drops `COMPOSER` or `FOOTER`, and dimensions below the floor raise `ValueError`. | `brain/ui/layout.py` | `agent_layout.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UI-23 | Engineering hypothesis (Operator TUI Agent-Style Layout) | Scripted agent-style interaction walk is inspectable. | A scripted agent-style operator interaction (type `/queue ...`, press Enter, type `/step`, press Enter, type `/state`, `/tick`, `/help`, `/quit`) over a deterministic injected tick client records the sequence of `ComposerAction` transitions, parsed `Command` records, dispatched `OperatorSession` routes, transcript appends, view transitions, and absence of kernel-boundary leaks; the row is OBSERVED and cannot fail the runner. | `brain/ui/tui.py` | `agent_tui_smoke.py` | OBSERVED |

### Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor developmental invariants

These rows are Phase 3.5 engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for a bounded local Expression + ReadabilityPredictor layer over Phase 3.1–3.4 developmental histories (`OutputHistory`, `WorldletHistory`, `ProtoBasicHistory`) and the Operator TUI transcript (`OperatorTranscript`). They are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize real LLM calls, a social/language harness, a natural-language teacher/corrector, Mode B reflective planning, real host execution, expression UI integration (deferred per `C10-AMEND-01`), `PerceptEvent` / `tick()` promotion of expression evidence, or any TLICA runtime mutation. Expression is a bounded local representation of how an existing local-history item is shaped for inspection — it is not language, not a generated utterance, not a chat/message/dialogue surface. `ReadabilityScore` is a `Fraction` in `[0, 1]` computed by a deterministic `Fraction`-only combinator over an `ExpressionFeatureVector`; it is not truth, validity, language quality, social success, intelligence, or agency.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-EXP-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | `ExpressionSource` is a finite closed enumeration. | `ExpressionSource` exposes exactly the documented members (`OUTPUT_HISTORY`, `WORLDLET_HISTORY`, `PROTO_BASIC_HISTORY`, `OPERATOR_TRANSCRIPT`); construction with any other kind raises and no callable, file path, network endpoint, or arbitrary identifier is accepted. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `expression_source_enum_closed.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-EXP-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | `ExpressionItem.text` is bounded printable. | Construction requires a printable `text` whose length is at most `EXPRESSION_TEXT_MAX_LEN`, a printable `item_id`, a known `ExpressionSource`, and bounded token counts; empty, non-printable, or over-length text raises `ValueError` naming I-EXP-02 and no silent truncation occurs. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `expression_item_bounded.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-EXP-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | `ExpressionFeatureVector` is deterministic and exact. | For the same `ExpressionItem`, `extract_features(item)` returns equal `ExpressionFeatureVector` records across repeated calls; every field is an exact `int` count or a `Fraction` ratio, with no float arithmetic, no `round`, no `math.*`, and no nondeterministic data source on the score path. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `expression_feature_vector_exact.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-EXP-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | `ReadabilityScore` is a `Fraction` in `[0, 1]`. | `ReadabilityScore.value` is a `Fraction`; construction with a value outside `[0, 1]` raises `ValueError` naming I-EXP-04 with no silent clamping; the predictor's score path uses only `Fraction` arithmetic. This module computes a bounded structural score over a local expression item. It does NOT model language. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `readability_score_fraction_bounded.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-EXP-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | `ReadabilityPrediction` is source-tagged and predictor-tagged. | Every `ReadabilityPrediction` carries the originating `ExpressionItem.item_id`, its `ExpressionSource`, a printable bounded `predictor_id`, and a bounded `ReadabilityScore`; predictions are frozen records, hold no callable, file handle, socket, LLM client, or path object, and are never written to a trace event, scenario file, source-history entry, or catalog file. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `readability_prediction_tagged.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-EXP-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | `ExpressionHistory` is copy-on-write and bounded. | `ExpressionHistory.append(record)` returns a new `ExpressionHistory` with prior `records` preserved exactly and the new record appended; when `len(records) >= EXPRESSION_HISTORY_MAX_ENTRIES` the oldest record is dropped before append; the history holds no callable, file handle, socket, LLM client, or path object, is never written to a trace event, scenario file, `OutputHistory` / `WorldletHistory` / `ProtoBasicHistory` / `OperatorTranscript` entry, or catalog file, and is process-local. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `expression_history_cow_bounded.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-EXP-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | Expression / readability operations do not mutate `BrainState` / MSI / PtCns / registry. | Before and after `extract_features`, `predict_readability`, `make_expression_record`, and `ExpressionHistory.append`, profile / MSI / PtCns / content registry identities and serializations are unchanged; no `tick()` is called and no `PerceptEvent` is emitted. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `expression_no_brainstate_mutation.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-EXP-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | Expression / readability operations do not mutate `OutputHistory` / `WorldletHistory` / `ProtoBasicHistory` / `OperatorTranscript`. | Before and after every expression bridge call from the source histories, the source-history identities, lengths, and entry tuples are unchanged; bridge constructors copy printable text out of source records and never call any source-history mutator. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `expression_no_source_history_mutation.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-EXP-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | Anti-Goodhart: empty / whitespace-only items score `Fraction(0)`. | For an `ExpressionItem` whose printable text is empty after whitespace normalization, `predict_readability(item)` returns a `ReadabilityPrediction` whose `score.value == Fraction(0)`; no path inflates a whitespace-only item above zero. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `readability_predictor_empty_item.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-EXP-10 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | Anti-Goodhart: repetition alone never increases the score. | For an `ExpressionItem` whose text is one repeated token (or character) of arbitrary count up to `EXPRESSION_TEXT_MAX_LEN`, the predicted score is non-increasing as the repeat count grows; the predictor weights distinct tokens positively and pure-repeat content cannot exceed the score of a single instance. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `readability_predictor_repetition_only.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-EXP-11 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | Anti-Goodhart: length alone is capped. | Beyond a fixed `LENGTH_SATURATION_BOUND`, the predicted score's length component is constant; arbitrary printable padding cannot push the total above the bound implied by shape and distinct-token components, and the predictor never exceeds `Fraction(1)`. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `readability_predictor_length_cap.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-EXP-12 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | Predictor determinism. | For the same `ExpressionItem`, `predict_readability(item)` returns predictions whose `score.value` is equal `Fraction` across repeated calls; no randomness, environment variable, time source, network call, or filesystem read participates in the score path. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `readability_predictor_determinism.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-EXP-13 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | Expression module has no I/O / network / file / shell import. | A static AST audit over `brain/development/expression.py` rejects imports of `os`, `os.system`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `pathlib`, `tempfile`, `shutil`, `brain.llm`, `brain.tlica`, `brain.tick`, and `curses`; the audit is local to the fixture and does not extend `tools.import_audit`. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `expression_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-EXP-14 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | Expression records are frozen dataclasses. | `ExpressionItem`, `ExpressionFeatureVector`, `ExpressionRecord`, `ReadabilityScore`, `ReadabilityPrediction`, and `ExpressionHistory` are immutable records (frozen dataclasses or equivalent); fields are bounded primitives, tuples of bounded primitives, `Fraction`, or other frozen expression records; no mutable kernel container is stored on these records. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `expression_feature_vector_exact.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-EXP-15 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | Bridge constructors are pure and do not register callbacks. | A static AST audit over `brain/development/expression.py` rejects module-level side effects, registry mutations, callback registrations, `atexit` handlers, decorator-installed hooks reaching into `brain/ui/`, `brain/tlica/`, `brain/llm/`, `brain/tick.py`, or source histories; bridge constructors (`expression_record_from_output_entry`, `_from_worldlet_response`, `_from_proto_basic_history`, `_from_operator_transcript`) read source records and return new `ExpressionItem` / `ExpressionRecord` values without calling any source-history mutator. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `expression_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-EXP-16 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | Predictor module has no `float` / `math` / `round` on the score path. | A static AST audit over `brain/development/expression.py` rejects `float(...)`, `round(...)`, and any `math.*` call inside any function transitively reachable from `predict_readability` and from `ReadabilityScore` construction; the score path uses only `int` and `Fraction` arithmetic. | `brain/development/expression.py` | `expression_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-EXP-17 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | Aggregate `ExpressionHistory` summary view is inspectable. | A summary view of `ExpressionHistory` records source-tagged counts, mean / min / max scores expressed exactly as `Fraction`, and an anti-Goodhart sketch under repeated / length-padded / whitespace-only items; the row is OBSERVED and cannot fail the runner. The summary view does not mutate any source history and is documented in `docs/campaigns/archive/PHASE3_5_EXPRESSION_READABILITY_AUDIT.md`. | `brain/development/expression.py` | (none) | OBSERVED |
| I-EXP-18 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.5 Expression + ReadabilityPredictor) | `ExpressionHistory` write-to-disk path is NOT-EXERCISED. | No Phase 3.5 `ExpressionHistory` serialization, save, export, or write-to-disk path exists in this campaign; any future write path requires an explicit reviewed policy artifact, dedicated catalog rows that constrain the path, fixtures that exercise the path under bounded conditions, and a stop condition for failure modes; this row exists so a future campaign cannot quietly add filesystem writes from expression evidence without registering coverage. | `brain/development/expression.py` | (none) | NOT-EXERCISED |

### Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection developmental invariants

These rows are Phase 3.6 engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for a bounded local Reflective Inspection layer that walks existing Phase 3.1–3.5 developmental histories (`OutputHistory`, `WorldletHistory`, `ProtoBasicHistory`, `ExpressionHistory`) and the Operator TUI transcript (`OperatorTranscript`) into read-only summary records. They are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize Mode B planning, self-modification, language/social communication, model-backed scoring, natural-language teacher/corrector, real host execution, reflective UI integration (deferred to Phase 3.8 per analog `C13-AMEND-01`), reflective serialization, weaving into traces or scenarios, an aggregate "quality" / "intelligence" / "social-success" score, `PerceptEvent` / `tick()` promotion of reflective evidence, or any TLICA runtime mutation. The reflective layer surfaces counts and source-supplied exact statistics; it does NOT produce an aggregate score, quality estimate, intelligence measure, social-success measure, or truth claim.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-REF-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | `ReflectiveSource` is a finite closed enumeration. | `ReflectiveSource` exposes exactly the documented members (`OUTPUT_HISTORY`, `WORLDLET_HISTORY`, `PROTO_BASIC_HISTORY`, `EXPRESSION_HISTORY`, `OPERATOR_TRANSCRIPT`); construction with any other kind raises and no callable, file path, network endpoint, or arbitrary identifier is accepted. | `brain/development/reflective.py` | `reflective_source_enum_closed.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REF-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | `ReflectiveSummaryItem` is bounded. | Construction requires a known `ReflectiveSource`, a bounded printable `summary_id`, an `entry_count` that is a non-negative `int`, a `counts_by_category` mapping with at most `REFLECTIVE_NOTES_MAX_NOTES` entries each bounded printable, exact `Fraction` source-supplied statistics, and a bounded printable `notes` tuple of at most `REFLECTIVE_NOTES_MAX_NOTES` entries each at most `REFLECTIVE_NOTES_MAX_LEN` characters; over-bound or non-printable inputs raise `ValueError` naming I-REF-02. | `brain/development/reflective.py` | `reflective_summary_item_bounded.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REF-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | `counts_by_category` sums exactly to `entry_count`. | For every `ReflectiveSummaryItem`, `sum(item.counts_by_category.values()) == item.entry_count`; mismatched totals raise `ValueError` naming I-REF-03. | `brain/development/reflective.py` | `reflective_summary_item_bounded.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REF-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | `distinct_id_count` cannot exceed `entry_count`. | For every `ReflectiveSummaryItem`, `item.distinct_id_count <= item.entry_count`; violations raise `ValueError` naming I-REF-04. | `brain/development/reflective.py` | `reflective_summary_item_bounded.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REF-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | `ReflectiveInspectionSnapshot` construction is deterministic. | For the same source histories, `make_reflective_snapshot(...)` returns equal `ReflectiveInspectionSnapshot` records across repeated calls; the snapshot is a frozen record holding only `ReflectiveSummaryItem` tuples and bounded primitives; no float arithmetic, no `round`, no `math.*`, no environment variable, no time source, no network call, and no filesystem read participate in construction. | `brain/development/reflective.py` | `reflective_snapshot_deterministic.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REF-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | Reflective operations do not mutate `BrainState` / MSI / PtCns / registry. | Before and after `make_reflective_snapshot(...)` and `make_reflective_summary(...)`, profile / MSI / PtCns / content registry identities and serializations are unchanged; no `tick()` is called and no `PerceptEvent` is emitted. | `brain/development/reflective.py` | `reflective_no_brainstate_mutation.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REF-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | Reflective operations do not mutate source histories. | Before and after every reflective construction call from the source histories (`OutputHistory`, `WorldletHistory`, `ProtoBasicHistory`, `ExpressionHistory`, `OperatorTranscript`), the source-history identities, lengths, and entry tuples are unchanged; reflective constructors copy bounded values out of source records and never call any source-history mutator. | `brain/development/reflective.py` | `reflective_no_source_history_mutation.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REF-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | Reflective summary surfaces source-supplied scores only; no aggregate score is produced. The reflective layer surfaces counts and source-supplied exact statistics; it does NOT produce an aggregate score, quality estimate, intelligence measure, social-success measure, or truth claim. | `ReflectiveSummaryItem` and `ReflectiveInspectionSnapshot` expose exact counts and `Fraction` statistics drawn directly from source records (e.g. existing `ReadabilityScore` values); no aggregate score, quality estimate, intelligence measure, social-success measure, or truth claim is constructed; no reflective field is named "score", "quality", "intelligence", or "social_success" without explicit source-supplied passthrough tagging. | `brain/development/reflective.py` | `reflective_no_aggregate_score.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-REF-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | Reflective module has no I/O / network / file / shell / LLM / TLICA / tick / curses import. | A static AST audit over `brain/development/reflective.py` rejects imports of `os`, `os.system`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `pathlib`, `tempfile`, `shutil`, `brain.llm`, `brain.tlica`, `brain.tick`, and `curses`; the audit is local to the fixture and does not extend `tools.import_audit`. | `brain/development/reflective.py` | `reflective_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-REF-10 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | Reflective records are frozen dataclasses. | `ReflectiveSummaryItem`, `ReflectiveInspectionSnapshot`, and `ReflectiveInspectionSummary` are immutable records (frozen dataclasses or equivalent); fields are bounded primitives, tuples of bounded primitives, `Fraction`, or other frozen reflective records; no mutable kernel container is stored on these records. | `brain/development/reflective.py` | `reflective_summary_item_bounded.py` + `reflective_snapshot_deterministic.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-REF-11 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | Reflective module has no `float` / `round` / `math` on the count / statistic path. | A static AST audit over `brain/development/reflective.py` rejects `float(...)`, `round(...)`, and any `math.*` call inside any function transitively reachable from `make_reflective_snapshot`, `make_reflective_summary`, and `ReflectiveSummaryItem` construction; the count / statistic path uses only `int` and `Fraction` arithmetic. | `brain/development/reflective.py` | `reflective_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-REF-12 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | Reflective constructors are pure and register no callbacks. | A static AST audit over `brain/development/reflective.py` rejects module-level side effects, registry mutations, callback registrations, `atexit` handlers, and decorator-installed hooks reaching into `brain/ui/`, `brain/tlica/`, `brain/llm/`, `brain/tick.py`, or source histories; reflective constructors read source records and return new `ReflectiveSummaryItem` / `ReflectiveInspectionSnapshot` values without calling any source-history mutator. | `brain/development/reflective.py` | `reflective_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-REF-13 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.6 Reflective Inspection) | Aggregate `ReflectiveInspectionSummary` walk is inspectable. | A summary view of `ReflectiveInspectionSnapshot` records source-tagged counts, distinct-id counts, source-supplied `Fraction` statistics where available, and an anti-Goodhart sketch under empty / repeated source histories; the row is OBSERVED and cannot fail the runner. ### Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress developmental invariants

These rows are Phase 3.7 engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for a bounded local Text Stream Ingress substrate over operator / system / probe-echo / generated raw text. They are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize Mode B planning, self-modification, language/social communication, natural-language teacher/corrector, real LLM calls (the explicit Phase 3.8b LLM Runtime Toggle owns the model-backed seam), real host execution, text-stream UI integration (deferred to Phase 3.8 per analog `C13-AMEND-01`), text-stream serialization or weaving into traces or scenarios, an aggregate "quality" / "intelligence" / "social-success" score, `PerceptEvent` / `tick()` promotion of text-stream evidence outside the explicit Phase 3.8 `/stream-promote` route, or any TLICA runtime mutation. The text-stream substrate surfaces bounded raw text evidence; it does NOT produce parse trees, language meaning, truth claims, `PRESERVE` / `DAMAGE` judgments, agency witnesses, or aggregate quality scores.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-STRM-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress) | `TextStreamSource` is a finite closed enumeration. | `TextStreamSource` exposes exactly the documented members (`OPERATOR`, `SYSTEM`, `PROBE_ECHO`, `GENERATED`); construction with any other kind raises and no callable, file path, network endpoint, or arbitrary identifier is accepted. | `brain/development/text_stream.py` | `text_stream_source_enum_closed.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-STRM-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress) | `TextStreamChunk` is bounded printable text and rejects `COGITO_ID` on every identifier and on text. | Construction requires a printable `text` whose length is at most `STREAM_TEXT_MAX_LEN`, a printable `chunk_id` distinct from `COGITO_ID`, a known `TextStreamSource`, and a printable bounded `provenance` whose length is at most `STREAM_PROVENANCE_MAX_LEN`; empty, non-printable, over-length, or `COGITO_ID`-equal text or identifier raises `ValueError` naming I-STRM-02 and no silent truncation occurs. | `brain/development/text_stream.py` | `text_stream_chunk_bounded.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-STRM-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress) | `TextStreamHistory` is copy-on-write and bounded. | `TextStreamHistory.append(chunk)` returns a new `TextStreamHistory` with prior `chunks` preserved exactly and the new chunk appended; when `len(chunks) >= STREAM_HISTORY_MAX_CHUNKS` the oldest chunk is dropped before append; the history holds no callable, file handle, socket, LLM client, or path object, is never written to a trace event, scenario file, source-history entry, or catalog file, and is process-local. | `brain/development/text_stream.py` | `text_stream_history_cow_bounded.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-STRM-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress) | `StreamFeatureVector` is deterministic and exact. | For the same `TextStreamChunk`, `extract_stream_features(chunk)` returns equal `StreamFeatureVector` records across repeated calls; every field is an exact `int` count or a `Fraction` ratio, with no `float` arithmetic, no `round`, no `math.*`, and no nondeterministic data source on the count / statistic path. | `brain/development/text_stream.py` | `text_stream_feature_vector_exact.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-STRM-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress) | `SegmentCandidate` is a structural span over a closed vocabulary. | `SegmentCandidate` carries a printable bounded `candidate_id`, a `segment_kind` in the closed vocabulary `("line", "delimited_span", "whitespace_run")`, integer `start` and `end` satisfying `0 <= start <= end <= len(chunk.text)`, and no payload text, parse tree, AST, semantic value, language label, truth flag, or readability score; `extract_segment_candidates(chunk)` returns at most `STREAM_SEGMENTS_MAX` candidates deterministically for a given chunk. | `brain/development/text_stream.py` | `text_stream_segment_candidate.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-STRM-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress) | `StreamPattern` requires `recurrence_count >= STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MIN`. StreamPattern is recurrence-backed structural evidence. | I-STRM-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress) | `StreamPromotionCandidate` requires explicit non-reserved `target_content_id` and explicit source / provenance / chunk_id and is not a `PerceptEvent`. StreamPromotionCandidate is not a PerceptEvent. The substrate never appends candidates to OperatorSession.event_queue and never calls tick(). The Phase 3.8 /stream-promote route owns event-queue append. | Construction requires a printable bounded `candidate_id`, a `target_content_id` distinct from `COGITO_ID` and from every reserved sentinel, a known `TextStreamSource`, a printable bounded `chunk_id` (caller contract), a printable bounded `text` whose length is at most `STREAM_TEXT_MAX_LEN`, an optional `pattern_id` referencing a known `StreamPattern`, and a printable bounded `provenance` whose length is at most `STREAM_PROVENANCE_MAX_LEN`; missing provenance, missing `chunk_id`, missing source, reserved `target_content_id`, non-printable or over-length text, or violation of any of the above raises `ValueError` naming I-STRM-07; the resulting record is not a `PerceptEvent`, exposes no `Act` / `ModeOp` / `AgencyWitness` / `tick` callback / `feasibleProjectedPCE` / event-queue field, and is not added to any event queue by the substrate. | `brain/development/text_stream.py` | `text_stream_promotion_candidate.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-STRM-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress) | Text-stream operations do not mutate `BrainState` / MSI / PtCns / registry. | Before and after `make_text_stream_chunk`, `TextStreamHistory.append`, `extract_stream_features`, `extract_segment_candidates`, `make_stream_pattern`, and `make_stream_promotion_candidate`, profile / MSI / PtCns / content registry identities and serializations are unchanged; no `tick()` is called and no `PerceptEvent` is emitted. | `brain/development/text_stream.py` | `text_stream_no_brainstate_mutation.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-STRM-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress) | Text-stream operations do not mutate any existing source history (`OutputHistory` / `WorldletHistory` / `ProtoBasicHistory` / `ExpressionHistory` / `OperatorTranscript`). | Before and after every text-stream construction call from the source histories, the source-history identities, lengths, and entry tuples are unchanged; text-stream constructors copy bounded printable text out of source records and never call any source-history mutator. | `brain/development/text_stream.py` | `text_stream_no_source_history_mutation.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-STRM-10 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress) | Text-stream operations do not call `tick()` and do not append to `OperatorSession.event_queue`; promotion is the Phase 3.8 `/stream-promote` route only. | `brain/development/text_stream.py` calls no `tick()`, emits no `PerceptEvent`, and never appends to `OperatorSession.event_queue`; `make_stream_promotion_candidate` returns a `StreamPromotionCandidate` record without invoking the event queue or `tick` path; the fixture asserts these properties by static AST audit and by before/after identity checks of `OperatorSession.event_queue` over a deterministic walk. | `brain/development/text_stream.py` | `text_stream_no_tick.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-STRM-11 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress) | Anti-growth: repeated / huge chunks do not inflate `recurrence_count` above `STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX`, and no silent truncation occurs on the chunk text path. | Repeated identical chunks update a `StreamPattern` whose `recurrence_count` saturates at `STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX`; arbitrary repetition cannot exceed that bound; chunks whose text length exceeds `STREAM_TEXT_MAX_LEN` raise `ValueError` naming I-STRM-11 instead of being silently truncated; the count / statistic path uses only `int` and `Fraction` arithmetic. | `brain/development/text_stream.py` | `text_stream_anti_growth.py` | REQUIRED |

### Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction UI invariants

These rows are Phase 3.8 engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for an Operator Stream Interaction UI surface that extends the existing Operator TUI parser, session, snapshot, and render paths with a finite typed route over the accepted Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress substrate. They are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize Mode B planning, self-modification, social/language harnesses, natural-language teacher/corrector, real LLM calls (the explicit Phase 3.8b LLM Runtime Toggle owns the model-backed seam), real host execution, text-stream serialization or weaving into traces or scenarios, an aggregate "quality" / "intelligence" / "social-success" score, automatic promotion, or any TLICA runtime mutation. The Phase 3.8 stream surface appends bounded operator text to session-local `TextStreamHistory`, exposes read-only summary and candidate views over the Phase 3.7 substrate, and queues exactly one explicit `StreamPromotionCandidate` per `/stream-promote` call through the existing `OperatorEventQueue` surface; `/step` remains the only route that calls `tick()`. The stream surface produces no parse trees, no language meaning, no truth claims, no `PRESERVE` / `DAMAGE` judgments, no agency witnesses, no second classification paths, and no aggregate quality scores.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-UISTRM-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream command parser is finite and typed. | `LocalCommandLine.parse(line)` accepts exactly `/stream`, `/stream-summary`, `/stream-candidates`, and `/stream-promote` in addition to the existing approved verbs; each verb maps to a fixed `OperatorCommand` and a frozen `Command` payload; lines beginning with any other token, missing required arguments, or carrying non-printable / over-bound text return a `LocalCommandError` with bounded printable text without reaching `OperatorSession.event_queue` or `OperatorSession` stream state. | `brain/ui/command_line.py` | `stream_command_parser.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream command payloads are bounded and constructor-checked. | `/stream` text is non-empty bounded printable raw text compatible with `TextStreamChunk` (length at most `STREAM_TEXT_MAX_LEN`); `/stream-promote` `candidate_id` is bounded printable text (length at most `STREAM_PROMOTION_MAX`); stream command payload records are frozen and carry no callable, file handle, socket, LLM client, subprocess handle, or path object; payload construction with empty, non-printable, over-length, or `COGITO_ID`-equal values raises `ValueError` or returns `LocalCommandError` without partially mutating session state. | `brain/ui/command_line.py` | `stream_command_parser.py` | REQUIRED |

| I-UISTRM-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | `/stream-candidates` is read-only. | Dispatching `OperatorCommand.INSPECT_STREAM_CANDIDATES` selects a stream-candidate view on `OperatorSession` and may build immutable candidate snapshots from `SegmentCandidate`, `StreamPattern`, and `StreamPromotionCandidate` records derived from local stream history; before and after dispatch, local stream history, candidate records, `BrainState`, source histories, `OperatorSession.event_queue`, `latest_tick`, and `tick_counter` are unchanged; the dispatch never calls `tick()`. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `stream_summary_candidates.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | `/stream-promote` queues exactly one validated candidate and does not tick. | Dispatching `OperatorCommand.STREAM_PROMOTE` resolves exactly one explicit `StreamPromotionCandidate` by `candidate_id`, converts it to one `QueuePerceptPayload` through the same constructor-bounded path used by `/queue` (`PerceptEvent`-constructor checked, non-reserved `target_content_id`, bounded printable text, no callable / resource / client fields), and enqueues it through `OperatorEventQueue.enqueue`; the dispatch does not call `tick()`, does not call `dequeue`, does not append to private queue storage directly, does not mutate `BrainState`, `latest_tick`, or `tick_counter`, and leaves `OperatorSession.event_queue` length increased by exactly one on success. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `stream_promotion_queue.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | `/step` remains the only stream interaction path that calls `tick()`. | Across `/stream`, `/stream-summary`, `/stream-candidates`, and `/stream-promote` dispatches, `OperatorSession.tick_counter`, `OperatorSession.latest_tick`, and the underlying `BrainState` identity are unchanged; only `OperatorCommand.STEP_TICK` reaches the existing `_dispatch_step` route that invokes the public `tick()` entrypoint with the queued events and current `BrainState`. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `stream_tick_boundary.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream command failure paths are local UI status/error only. | For malformed `/stream` input, over-bound `/stream` text, non-printable text, unknown `/stream-promote` `candidate_id`, candidate-to-payload constructor rejection, `PerceptEvent` validation failure, and a full `OperatorEventQueue`, the router records the failure as bounded local UI status/error text on `OperatorSession` and leaves `BrainState`, `ScalarProfile`, `MSI`, `PtCns`, `ContentRegistry`, `latest_tick`, `tick_counter`, source histories, `OperatorTranscript`, and `OperatorSession.event_queue` length unchanged; only successful `/stream-promote` increases `OperatorSession.event_queue` length by exactly one. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `stream_failure_isolation.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream snapshots and render output are deterministic and read-only. | For equal stream interaction state and equal view-model inputs, stream-summary and stream-candidate snapshots and rendered rows are equal across repeated calls; snapshot construction and rendering mutate no `TextStreamHistory`, no `StreamPromotionCandidate` record, no `BrainState`, no source history, no `OperatorSession.event_queue`, no trace event, no scenario file, and no catalog file; rendering performs no curses call from pure snapshot/render paths and no file or network I/O. | `brain/ui/snapshot.py` + `brain/ui/render.py` | `stream_snapshot_render.py` | REQUIRED |

### Phase 3.8b LLM Runtime Toggle UI invariants

These rows are Phase 3.8b engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for an explicit operator-facing LLM Runtime Toggle that adds one CLI surface (`--llm-mode <mode>`) plus a small typed helper module (`brain/ui/llm_runtime.py`) on top of the existing `LLMClient` protocol and the existing `tick(..., client, ...)` seam. They are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize a non-offline default, automatic credential / tool detection without opt-in, an environment read inside `build_llm_client_from_config`, a new `LLMClient` implementation beyond the four shipped backends, a second classification path alongside the existing `tick()` route, model-backed scoring of stream evidence, model output reaching traces / scenarios / source histories, a new `tick()` argument signature, mid-session mode flips, a curses key binding for mode selection, an implicit cache enable, or any TLICA runtime mutation. The toggle surfaces a finite closed `LlmRuntimeMode` (`OFFLINE`, `MOCK`, `ANTHROPIC_API`, `CLAUDE_CLI`); a frozen / slots-bearing `LlmRuntimeConfig`; a `parse_llm_runtime_args(argv, env)` parser that resolves `api_key` from CLI then `BRAIN_ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` then `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` (supplied env only); a `build_llm_client_from_config(config)` factory that never reads `os.environ`, raises `LlmRuntimeError` locally before launch when the explicit config is insufficient, and returns an `LLMClient`-compatible client (or a `CachedClient` wrapping the backend when caching is opt-in for `ANTHROPIC_API` / `CLAUDE_CLI`); and the entrypoint plumbing that passes the resolved client into `run_curses(session, client=..., ...)` so the selected client enters the kernel through the existing `tick()` seam. Default behavior remains offline: every existing REQUIRED and STRUCTURAL fixture passes with no `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`, no `BRAIN_ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`, and no `claude` executable on PATH. The optional real model-backed smoke walk is OBSERVED and cannot fail the runner; the LLM runtime save / export path is NOT-EXERCISED. The toggle introduces no parse trees, no language meaning, no truth claims, no `PRESERVE` / `DAMAGE` judgments, no agency witnesses, no aggregate quality scores, no second classification path, and no automatic promotion.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-LLMTOG-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8b LLM Runtime Toggle) | Default `LlmRuntimeConfig()` builds `OfflineStandInClient`. | `LlmRuntimeConfig()` with no arguments produces a record whose `mode` is `LlmRuntimeMode.OFFLINE` and whose `enable_cache` is `False`; `build_llm_client_from_config(LlmRuntimeConfig())` returns an instance of `OfflineStandInClient` and does not consult `os.environ`. | `brain/ui/llm_runtime.py` | `llm_runtime_default_offline.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMTOG-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8b LLM Runtime Toggle) | `LlmRuntimeMode` is a finite closed enumeration. | `LlmRuntimeMode` exposes exactly `OFFLINE`, `MOCK`, `ANTHROPIC_API`, and `CLAUDE_CLI`; construction with any other value raises (or the parse helper raises `LlmRuntimeError`) before a config is built. | `brain/ui/llm_runtime.py` | `llm_runtime_mode_closed.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMTOG-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8b LLM Runtime Toggle) | Each accepted mode returns the expected concrete client type without invoking it. | `build_llm_client_from_config(<each mode>)` returns an instance whose class is the documented backend (`OfflineStandInClient`, `MockClient`, `AnthropicAPIClient`, `ClaudeCLIClient`), or a `CachedClient` wrapping the backend when caching is enabled; no HTTP / subprocess call is performed at factory time; for `CLAUDE_CLI` construction checks the fixture may pass `claude_cli_executable=sys.executable` or another guaranteed-present executable, and the fixture asserts construction only and must not invoke `eval_consistency`. | `brain/ui/llm_runtime.py` | `llm_runtime_factory_per_mode.py` | REQUIRED |

With `enable_cache=True` and `ANTHROPIC_API` / `CLAUDE_CLI`, the returned client is a `CachedClient` wrapping the expected backend, and the cache directory is the `brain/.llm_cache` default. | `brain/ui/llm_runtime.py` | `llm_runtime_cache_gated.py` | REQUIRED |
