The Step 8 behavior report exercises Growth Ledger emissions along the `/stream → /stream-promote → /step` route and may either promote this row in a follow-up catalog patch or leave it NOT-EXERCISED. | `brain/development/growth_ledger.py` | (none) | NOT-EXERCISED |

### Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline invariants

These rows are Phase 3.14 engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for a bounded, cataloged, observable LLM cache discipline that prevents repeated external model calls across ticks while preserving offline-as-default, explicit opt-in for model-backed modes, no hidden LLM calls, no unbounded new cache surface, and no tick semantic change. L0 (`LLMBackedPtCns._cache`) remains per-instance and `brain/tick.py` is untouched. L1 (`CachedClient` in `brain/llm/client.py`) is the existing prompt-hash transport cache; after a model-backed mode is explicitly selected, the runtime parser flips its default on. A new `--llm-disable-cache` flag forces L1 (and L2) off for model-backed modes; `--llm-enable-cache` remains accepted as an explicit affirmation; supplying both flags raises `LlmRuntimeError`. OFFLINE / MOCK still reject `--llm-enable-cache` and treat `--llm-disable-cache` as a no-op without unlocking cache access. L2 (the canonical semantic evaluation cache implemented inside `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` per Option 3 of the Step 5 plan) keys on the seven-tuple `(SEMANTIC_CACHE_SCHEMA_VERSION="llm-semantic-cache-v1", PROMPT_TEMPLATE_VERSION="prompt-template-v1", PARSE_SCHEMA_VERSION="consistency-eval-v1", backend_family, model_identity, existing_msi_context, new_text)` with `existing_msi_context` a sorted tuple of `(content_id, text)` pairs over non-cogito MSI contents; the evaluated `new_id` is excluded from the key but retained in the rendered prompt. L2 entries store only `{"key_prefix", "parsed"}`; raw prompt, raw response, error text, and provider metadata are never persisted to L2 files. L2 is capped at `SEMANTIC_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES = 1024`; at cap, hits read but misses do not write (emitting `llm.semantic_cache_skip` with `reason="capacity"`). Corrupt L1 / L2 entries fail loud and never silently call the inner client. Parse failures, provider failures, timeouts, refusals, schema mismatches, and corrupt entries never become L2 success hits; retries exhausted without a parse-success emit `llm.semantic_cache_skip` with `reason="parse_failure"`. Cache hit / miss / store / skip events are observable through `CognitionTracer` (`llm.cache_hit`, `llm.cache_miss`, `llm.semantic_cache_hit`, `llm.semantic_cache_miss`, `llm.semantic_cache_store`, `llm.semantic_cache_skip`); trace payloads carry only `content_id`, the 8-character `key_prefix`, and `reason` — never raw prompt or raw response. Dependency direction is one-way: `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` does not import `brain.ui.*` or `brain.tick`. The L2 directory is `brain/.llm_cache/eval_v1/`, covered by the existing gitignored `brain/.llm_cache/` root. These rows are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize Mode B planning, self-modification, social/language harnesses, natural-language teacher/corrector, real LLM calls beyond the existing Phase 3.8b LLM Runtime Toggle and Phase 3.11 Codex CLI Runtime Option seams, real host execution, persistence schema changes, `/save-session` / `/load-session` extensions, `/growth-ledger` UI surfaces, SelfModel implementation, or any TLICA runtime mutation. "Semantic" in "semantic evaluation cache" is engineering language about cache identity, not a claim that ToyI understands meaning. Phase 3.14 introduces no new L1 cache surface; flipping `enable_cache=True` by default activates the existing v0.16 `CachedClient`, so "no unbounded new cache" is preserved (L1 bounding is tracked as DEFERRED under `I-LLMCACHE-20`). The end-to-end real-LLM cache smoke (`I-LLMCACHE-21`) and the end-to-end Phase 3.14 behavior probe (`I-LLMCACHE-22`) are NOT-EXERCISED in v1; Step 8's behavior report exercises L1 + L2 along the deterministic local-client route.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-LLMCACHE-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | L0 cache remains per-instance / per-tick and `brain/tick.py` is untouched. | A freshly constructed `LLMBackedPtCns` starts with `_cache == {COGITO_ID: PRESERVE}`. `brain/tick.py` references none of `SEMANTIC_CACHE_DIR`, `SEMANTIC_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES`, `SEMANTIC_CACHE_SCHEMA_VERSION`, `_l2_dir`, `_l2_lookup`, or `_l2_store`. The L0 cache is not promoted to a shared store, not persisted across ticks, and not exposed through `tick()`. | `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py`, `brain/tick.py` | `llm_cache_no_tick_change.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | Model-backed modes enable L1 transport cache by default after explicit model-backed opt-in; offline remains default. | `parse_llm_runtime_args([], {})` resolves `mode == OFFLINE` and `enable_cache == False`. `parse_llm_runtime_args(["--llm-mode", m], {})` for `m in {"anthropic-api", "claude-cli", "codex-cli"}` resolves `enable_cache == True`. `BRAIN_LLM_MODE` env override flips cache on identically. `parse_llm_runtime_args(["--llm-mode", "mock"], {})` keeps `enable_cache == False`. `build_llm_client_from_config` under the parsed default for `codex-cli` produces `CachedClient` wrapping `CodexCLIClient`. | `brain/ui/llm_runtime.py` | `llm_cache_runtime_policy.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | `--llm-disable-cache` disables cache for model-backed modes; `--llm-enable-cache` remains compatible affirmation; conflicting flags raise. | `parse_llm_runtime_args(["--llm-mode", "codex-cli", "--llm-disable-cache"], {}).enable_cache is False`; `parse_llm_runtime_args(["--llm-mode", "codex-cli", "--llm-enable-cache"], {}).enable_cache is True`. Supplying both `--llm-enable-cache` and `--llm-disable-cache` (in any order, in any mode) raises `LlmRuntimeError` whose message names both flag names. The factory under `codex-cli + --llm-disable-cache` returns a bare `CodexCLIClient` (no `CachedClient` wrap). | `brain/ui/llm_runtime.py` | `llm_cache_runtime_policy.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | OFFLINE / MOCK never read or write L1 / L2 cache files; `--llm-enable-cache` rejects for those modes; `--llm-disable-cache` is a no-op. | `build_llm_client_from_config(LlmRuntimeConfig(mode=OFFLINE, enable_cache=True))` and the `MOCK` analogue raise `LlmRuntimeError` whose message names the mode. `parse_llm_runtime_args(["--llm-mode", "offline", "--llm-disable-cache"], {})` yields `enable_cache == False` and `build_llm_client_from_config(...)` returns `OfflineStandInClient`; the MOCK analogue returns `MockClient`. Neither path constructs `CachedClient` and the L2 surface `LLMBackedPtCns._derive_l2_metadata(client)` returns `None` for both. | `brain/ui/llm_runtime.py`, `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | `llm_cache_runtime_policy.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | L1 `CachedClient` semantics remain prompt-hash transport cache. | Two identical `eval_consistency(p)` calls against `CachedClient(counting_inner)` produce one inner call, one cache file under `cache_dir`, and matching responses. The file name is `<sha256(prompt).hexdigest()>.json`. A different prompt produces a different file and a second inner call. The L1 entry schema and serialization are unchanged from v0.16. | `brain/llm/client.py` | `llm_cache_transport.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | L2 canonical evaluation cache is keyed by the locked semantic payload and excludes the evaluated `new_id`. | `LLMBackedPtCns.eval(content_id)` derives an L2 key from `(SEMANTIC_CACHE_SCHEMA_VERSION, PROMPT_TEMPLATE_VERSION, PARSE_SCHEMA_VERSION, backend_family, model_identity, existing_msi_context, new_text)` and looks up `<sha256_hex>.json` under `SEMANTIC_CACHE_DIR`. Two evaluations with the same `existing_msi_context` and same `new_text` but different `content_id` produce the same L2 key and the second call is an L2 hit (no inner call, one L2 entry). | `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | `llm_cache_semantic_key.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | L2 key namespace includes cache schema, prompt template, parse schema, backend family, and model identity. | `_canonical_l2_key(...)` is the SHA-256 hex of `repr(seven_tuple).encode("utf-8")` where the seven-tuple is exactly `(SEMANTIC_CACHE_SCHEMA_VERSION, PROMPT_TEMPLATE_VERSION, PARSE_SCHEMA_VERSION, backend_family, model_identity, existing_msi_context, new_text)`. Mutating any single one of `backend_family`, `model_identity`, `existing_msi_context`, or `new_text` produces a distinct 64-character hex key. The three module-level version constants are `"llm-semantic-cache-v1"`, `"prompt-template-v1"`, and `"consistency-eval-v1"`. | `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py`, `brain/llm/prompts.py`, `brain/llm/parse.py` | `llm_cache_semantic_key.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | L2 canonicalization preserves legitimate existing-MSI-context differences and reuses same-`new_text`/different-`new_id` results under the same context. | Two `LLMBackedPtCns` instances with the same `new_text` but different `existing_msi_context` produce different L2 keys and two L2 entries. Same `existing_msi_context` + same `new_text` under different `content_id` collapses to one L2 entry. `existing_msi_context` is built as a `tuple` of `(content_id, text)` pairs sorted by `content_id` ascending over non-cogito MSI members. | `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | `llm_cache_semantic_key.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | L2 stores only parse-success entries; failure classes are kept distinct. | When `LLMBackedPtCns.eval(...)` exhausts retries without a parse-success and raises the I-LLM-01 `ValueError`, no L2 entry is written for that key; the tracer records exactly one `llm.semantic_cache_skip` event with `reason="parse_failure"`. When `LLMBackedPtCns.eval(...)` succeeds after a retry, exactly one L2 entry is written whose JSON payload is `{"key_prefix", "parsed"}` and whose `parsed` value is the canonical `ConsistencyEval.name`. Provider failures, timeouts, refusals, schema mismatches, and corrupt entries never produce an L2 success hit; their handling does not collapse into a single cache state. | `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | `llm_cache_parse_failure.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-10 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | Corrupt L1 / L2 cache entries fail loud with bounded error and do not silently call inner. | A corrupt L1 entry (invalid JSON in `brain/.llm_cache/<sha256>.json`) makes `CachedClient.eval_consistency(...)` raise a `RuntimeError` whose message contains `"corrupt"` and does not call the inner client. A corrupt L2 entry (invalid JSON, unexpected key set, invalid `parsed` value, or `key_prefix` mismatch) makes `LLMBackedPtCns.eval(...)` raise a `RuntimeError` whose message contains `"corrupt"`; the inner client is not silently called. Bounded errors never carry raw prompt or raw response text. | `brain/llm/client.py`, `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | `llm_cache_parse_failure.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-11 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | L2 cache growth is bounded at `SEMANTIC_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES = 1024`. | When `len(list(SEMANTIC_CACHE_DIR.glob("*.json"))) >= 1024`, the next L2 miss does not write a new entry; the file count is unchanged after the call. The inner client may still be invoked (the explicit model-backed inner path is not blocked by cap), and exactly one `llm.semantic_cache_skip` event with `reason="capacity"` is emitted on the tracer. Below cap, a parse-success writes exactly one new L2 entry whose payload keys are exactly `{"key_prefix", "parsed"}`. No eviction or pruning policy fires in v1. | `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | `llm_cache_bounds_artifacts.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-12 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | L1 / L2 cache files are sensitive local artifacts; gitignored; no raw prompt / response appears in committed artifacts. | `SEMANTIC_CACHE_DIR == Path("brain/.llm_cache") / "eval_v1"`. The repo-root `.gitignore` covers `brain/.llm_cache/` (and therefore `eval_v1/`). A produced L2 entry has exactly the JSON keys `{"key_prefix", "parsed"}` with no `"prompt"`, `"response"`, `"raw"`, `"error"`, `"trace"`, or `"headers"` field. The L2 file name is a 64-character hex digest; no committed fixture or doc embeds raw prompt or raw response text. | `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py`, `.gitignore` | `llm_cache_bounds_artifacts.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-13 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | L1 / L2 observability emits bounded tracer events without raw prompt / response / secret / full key. | L1 emits `llm.cache_hit` / `llm.cache_miss` with payload `{cache_key_prefix}` (8 hex chars). L2 emits `llm.semantic_cache_hit`, `llm.semantic_cache_miss`, `llm.semantic_cache_store`, and `llm.semantic_cache_skip` with payload subset of `{content_id, key_prefix, reason}` (`key_prefix` is exactly 8 hex chars). No cache event payload contains keys `prompt`, `response`, `raw`, `error`, `secret`, `api_key`, `headers`, or `full_key`. No cache event payload string value contains representative raw text fixtures placed in the source. | `brain/llm/client.py`, `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py`, `brain/trace.py` | `llm_cache_observability.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-14 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | Cache hit path does not call inner client; miss path calls inner only in explicit model-backed mode. | After a first L1 miss + write, subsequent L1 lookups for the same prompt return the cached response without calling the inner client; `cache.hit_count` and `cache.miss_count` reflect the lookups exactly. A miss against `CachedClient` calls inner exactly once. The L2 surface is unreachable for OFFLINE / MOCK; in those modes `LLMBackedPtCns._l2_metadata is None` and `LLMBackedPtCns.eval(...)` does not touch the L2 directory. | `brain/llm/client.py`, `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | `llm_cache_transport.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-15 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | Different semantic contexts evaluate separately; no false hit across namespaces. | Mutating each L2 key field individually (`backend_family`, `model_identity`, `existing_msi_context`, `new_text`) yields a distinct SHA-256 hex key. Two LLMBackedPtCns instances built over the same `new_text`/`new_id` but different `existing_msi_context` produce two distinct L2 entries. No L2 lookup ever returns a hit derived from a different `backend_family`, `model_identity`, `prompt_template_version`, `parse_schema_version`, or `existing_msi_context`. | `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | `llm_cache_semantic_key.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-16 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | No `brain/tick.py` semantic change; cached and uncached evaluation preserve `(new_state, TickRecord)`. | `tick(state, [event], bare_client)` and `tick(state, [event], CachedClient(bare_client_with_same_response))` produce field-for-field equal `BrainState` (profile values + domain, MSI contents + threshold, ptcns eval map, registry texts) and field-for-field equal `TickRecord` (tick_index, profile_values, msi_contents, eval_map, boundary, mode_trace, triggered_mode, registry.texts, notes) for the same client responses. `brain/tick.py` source is unchanged. | `brain/tick.py`, `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | `llm_cache_no_tick_change.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-17 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | Static AST audit rejects hidden model-call / network / subprocess / filesystem mutation / raw prompt leakage / disallowed imports in the new L2 cache code path. | A static AST audit over `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` rejects imports of `brain.ui`, `brain.tick`, `brain.development`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `sqlite3`, `tempfile`, `shutil`, `atexit`, `threading`, `asyncio`, `signal`; rejects calls `eval`, `exec`, `compile`, `__import__`, `tick`, `save_session`, `load_session`, `maybe_autosave_after_mutation`, and any call whose dotted name starts with `subprocess.`, `socket.`, `urllib.`, `http.`, `sqlite3.`, `shutil.`, `tempfile.`, `atexit.`, `threading.`, `asyncio.`, `signal.`, `importlib.`, `os.system`, `os.popen`, `os.exec`, `os.spawn`. The `_l2_store` body source does not contain the literal payload-key strings `"prompt"`, `"response"`, `"raw"`, `"error"`, `"trace"`, `"headers"`. | `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | `llm_cache_static_audit.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-18 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | No cognitive / claim-boundary drift in the new cache code. | The inherited `brain.development.coherence_monitor._FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS` tuple (case-insensitive) does not appear on any source line of `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py`. The phrase "semantic cache key" / "semantic evaluation cache" refers to cache identity only and is never used to claim that ToyI understands meaning, truth, agency, or self-model. | `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | `llm_cache_static_audit.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-19 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | Cache dependency direction is one-way; no `brain.ui.*` imports inside `brain.llm.*` modules. | Every `*.py` module under `brain/llm/` is parsed; no import targets `brain.ui` or `brain.ui.*` or `brain.tick`. The L2 metadata derivation introspects the wrapped client by class name (`type(inner).__name__`) so the L2 surface never imports the runtime config module. | `brain/llm/*.py` | `llm_cache_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-LLMCACHE-20 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.15 L1 Cache Hygiene) | L1 cache bounding by `L1_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES = 1024` via write-skip-at-cap admission policy. | `CachedClient` admits at most `L1_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES` `*.json` entries under the cache directory. At cap, a miss does not write a new entry; existing entries remain present and readable; hits continue to read. The cache itself never evicts; only new admissions are skipped. `L1_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES == 1024`. After pre-filling the cache directory with `L1_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES` synthetic entries, an at-cap miss leaves the directory at exactly `L1_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES` files, every original entry is still present and readable, and existing entry contents are unchanged. | `brain/llm/client.py` | `llm_cache_l1_capacity.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-21 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | Real external model-backed cache smoke remains NOT-EXERCISED in v1. | No documented Phase 3.14 dry-run helper, OBSERVED summary view, or scripted operator walk executes a real model-backed cache run during the campaign. Any future end-to-end smoke requires an explicit reviewed policy artifact, a dedicated catalog row (promoted from NOT-EXERCISED to OBSERVED or REQUIRED), and a stop condition for failure modes. This row exists so a future campaign cannot quietly add a real-LLM cache walk without registering coverage. | `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | (none) | NOT-EXERCISED |
| I-LLMCACHE-22 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.14 LLM Cache Discipline) | Phase 3.14 end-to-end behavior probe is NOT-EXERCISED in v1. | The Step 8 behavior report exercises L1 + L2 along the deterministic local-client route only; no scripted operator walk against a real provider exists. A future campaign may promote this row in a follow-up catalog patch or leave it NOT-EXERCISED. | `brain/llm/ptcns_backed.py` | (none) | NOT-EXERCISED |
| I-LLMCACHE-23 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.15 L1 Cache Hygiene) | At-cap miss still calls the inner client; the response is still returned to the caller. | When `CachedClient.eval_consistency(prompt)` runs with the cache directory already at `L1_CACHE_MAX_ENTRIES` entries and `prompt` not previously cached, `inner.eval_consistency(prompt)` is called exactly once and its return value is returned to the caller unchanged. The cache write is the only operation that is skipped. | `brain/llm/client.py` | `llm_cache_l1_capacity.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-24 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.15 L1 Cache Hygiene) | At-cap skip is observable: `llm.cache_skip` event with payload exactly `{cache_key_prefix, reason}` and `reason="capacity"`; new `skip_count` counter. | An at-cap miss emits exactly one `llm.cache_skip` event through the supplied `CognitionTracer`. The payload keys are exactly `{"cache_key_prefix", "reason"}`; `reason == "capacity"`; `cache_key_prefix` is an 8-character string. `CachedClient.skip_count` is a public `int` attribute that increments by one on each at-cap skip; `hit_count` and `miss_count` remain public `int` attributes. The event payload contains no raw prompt and no raw response. | `brain/llm/client.py` | `llm_cache_l1_capacity.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-25 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.15 L1 Cache Hygiene) | No silent repair; corrupt-entry fail-loud preserved; no skip event emitted below cap. | The bounded admission policy does not mutate or delete any pre-existing `*.json` entry. Tampering a cache file's JSON content still causes `CachedClient.eval_consistency(prompt)` to raise `RuntimeError`; the inner client is not called as a silent fall-back from a corrupt-entry read. Below the cap, normal misses and hits do not emit `llm.cache_skip` and do not increment `skip_count`. | `brain/llm/client.py` | `llm_cache_l1_capacity.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-LLMCACHE-26 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.15 L1 Cache Hygiene) | Static AST audit over `brain/llm/client.py` rejects new forbidden imports and asserts the `llm.cache_skip` payload uses only `cache_key_prefix` and `reason`. | The static audit walks `brain/llm/client.py`, rejects any import whose target is or starts with `brain.ui`, `brain.tick`, `brain.development`, `socket`, `http`, `requests`, `sqlite3`, `tempfile`, `atexit`, `threading`, `asyncio`, or `signal`; rejects calls to `eval`, `exec`, `compile`, `__import__`, `tick`, `save_session`, `load_session`, `maybe_autosave_after_mutation`; and asserts that the literal `_tracer.record("llm.cache_skip", {...})` call's payload dict has keys exactly `{"cache_key_prefix", "reason"}`. The new L1 audit function is distinct from the existing `I-LLMCACHE-17` L2 audit by target path and label. | `brain/llm/client.py` | `llm_cache_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |

### Phase 3.18 Bounded Internal Processing Window invariants

| I-PWND-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.18 Bounded Internal Processing Window) | Architecture A: `OperatorSession._run_processing_window` fires up to `processing_window_size` internal rehearsals after a successful external `STREAM_APPEND`; recurrence climbs deterministically; the OFF state (size == 0) is a strict no-op. | After `OperatorSession(state=initial_state(), processing_window_size=N).dispatch(Command(STREAM_APPEND, payload=StreamAppendPayload(text=T)))` succeeds, the live `OperatorSession` has exactly `1 + N` chunks in `stream_history.chunks` whose `provenance` set equals `{"operator"} ∪ {f"internal_processing_window:{k}:rehearsal" for k in 1..N}`; the `pattern_ledger.entries` tuple has length exactly 1 (one entry per structural signature); that entry's `recurrence_count == min(STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MIN + N, STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX)`; `confidence == Fraction(recurrence_count, STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX)`; `evidence_chunk_ids` size equals `min(1 + N, PATTERN_LEDGER_EVIDENCE_MAX)`; `saturation_state == SATURATED` iff `recurrence_count >= STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX`. At `processing_window_size == 0` (OFF), exactly one operator-source chunk is present, the Pattern Ledger entry's `recurrence_count == STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MIN`, no chunk carries an `internal_processing_window:*` provenance, and the kernel-invariant `assert_state_invariants(state)` remains green throughout. | `brain/development/processing_window.py`, `brain/ui/session.py` | `processing_window_integration.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PWND-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.18 Bounded Internal Processing Window; Phase 3.19 + 3.20 emit-set widened) | Static AST audit over `brain/development/processing_window.py` plus structural assertions on `InternalEventSource` / `RehearsalStep` / `MODULE_PRODUCED_STRINGS` / `build_rehearsal_provenance`. | A static AST audit over `brain/development/processing_window.py` rejects every import whose target is or starts with `os`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `pathlib`, `tempfile`, `shutil`, `curses`, `brain.tick`, `brain.llm`, `brain.ui`, `brain.tlica` (other than `brain.tlica.profile` for `COGITO_ID`), `threading`, `asyncio`, `atexit`, `signal`, `importlib`, `math`, `hashlib`, `time`, `random`; rejects every call whose name is `eval`, `exec`, `compile`, `__import__`, `open`, `float`, `round` or whose dotted prefix is `importlib.`, `atexit.`, `signal.`, `math.`, `hashlib.`, `time.`, `random.`; permits only the allowed set `{__future__, dataclasses, enum, typing, brain.development.text_stream, brain.tlica.profile}`; restricts module-level statements to imports, constants, function defs, class defs, and a module docstring. `InternalEventSource` is a `(str, Enum)` subclass whose value set is exactly `{"rehearsal", "pledger_summary", "cohmon_summary"}`. `PROCESSING_WINDOW_SIZE_MAX == 255`, `PROCESSING_WINDOW_CALL_BUDGET_MAX == 65535`, `PROCESSING_WINDOW_PROVENANCE_PREFIX == "internal_processing_window"`. No string in `MODULE_PRODUCED_STRINGS` and no source line of `brain/development/processing_window.py` contains any term in `brain.development.coherence_monitor._FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS` (case-insensitive). Phase 3.20 widens the v1-emit set to `{REHEARSAL, PLEDGER_SUMMARY, COHMON_SUMMARY}`: `build_rehearsal_provenance(tick_index=k, source=InternalEventSource.REHEARSAL)`, `build_rehearsal_provenance(tick_index=k, source=InternalEventSource.PLEDGER_SUMMARY)`, AND `build_rehearsal_provenance(tick_index=k, source=InternalEventSource.COHMON_SUMMARY)` for `k in {1, 2, 3, 42, 255}` all produce strings that are bounded printable, under `STREAM_PROVENANCE_MAX_LEN`, and contain none of the forbidden non-claim terms. No `InternalEventSource` member is reserved at v0.28. `RehearsalStep` has `__slots__ == ("tick_index", "source", "provenance", "text")`; no slot's value is callable, exposes `eval_consistency` / `fileno` / `send_signal`. | `brain/development/processing_window.py` | `processing_window_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |

### Phase 3.19 Internal Feedback Loop invariants

| I-IFBK-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.19 Internal Feedback Loop) | Architecture B: `OperatorSession._run_processing_window` interleaves a pattern-ledger summary chunk after each rehearsal when `feedback_mode == FeedbackMode.PATTERN_LEDGER`; produces `1 + 2 * N` stream chunks, at least one second-order Pattern Ledger entry, deterministic recurrence accounting, kernel invariants green, zero real model calls. | After `OperatorSession(state=initial_state(), processing_window_size=N, feedback_mode=FeedbackMode.PATTERN_LEDGER).dispatch(Command(STREAM_APPEND, payload=StreamAppendPayload(text=T)))` succeeds, the live `OperatorSession` has exactly `1 + 2 * N` chunks in `stream_history.chunks` whose `provenance` set partitions as `{"operator"} ∪ {f"internal_processing_window:{k}:rehearsal" for k in 1..N} ∪ {f"internal_processing_window:{k}:pledger_summary" for k in 1..N}`; the `pattern_ledger.entries` tuple has length at least 2 (the seed entry plus at least one second-order summary entry whose `pattern_id` differs from the seed's `pattern_id`); the seed entry's `recurrence_count == min(STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MIN + N, STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX)`; the sum over all second-order entries of `(recurrence_count - STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MIN + 1)` equals exactly N (one observation per feedback chunk); every entry's bounded constructor invariants hold; `assert_state_invariants(state)` remains green; two independent fresh `OperatorSession` instances with identical inputs and configuration produce bit-identical `pattern_ledger.entries` pattern_id tuples, bit-identical per-entry `recurrence_count` tuples, and bit-identical `growth_ledger.events` event_id tuples (determinism). At `processing_window_size == 0`, `feedback_mode == FeedbackMode.PATTERN_LEDGER` is a strict no-op (one operator chunk; one Pattern Ledger entry at MIN). At `feedback_mode == FeedbackMode.OFF`, the path is bit-identical to the Phase 3.18 rehearsal-only behavior (no `pledger_summary` provenance appears; one Pattern Ledger entry). | `brain/development/processing_window.py`, `brain/ui/session.py` | `internal_feedback_integration.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-IFBK-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.19 Internal Feedback Loop; Phase 3.20 widened) | Constructor + non-claim audit on `FeedbackMode`, `validate_feedback_mode`, `build_pledger_summary_text`, the widened `_V1_EMITTED_SOURCES` emit set, and the `MODULE_PRODUCED_STRINGS` extension. | `FeedbackMode` is a `(str, Enum)` subclass whose value set is exactly `{"off", "pattern_ledger", "coherence", "pattern_and_coherence"}`. `validate_feedback_mode(member)` returns the same `FeedbackMode` member for every member; `validate_feedback_mode(bad)` raises `ValueError` for `bad` in `{"off", "pattern_ledger", "coherence", "pattern_and_coherence", 0, 1, True, False, None, (), [], object()}`. `build_pledger_summary_text(pattern_id, recurrence_count, saturation_state_value)` for `pattern_id in {"pledger:0000000000000000", "pledger:a5e6f92cd3330c9b", "pledger:ffffffffffffffff"}`, `recurrence_count in {0, 1, 2, 3, 42, 255, 256, 100}`, and `saturation_state_value in {"open", "saturated", "quiesced"}` produces strings that are bounded printable, start with `"pledger_summary "`, length `<= PLEDGER_SUMMARY_TEXT_MAX_LEN == 240`, length `<= STREAM_TEXT_MAX_LEN`, do not contain `COGITO_ID`, and do not contain any term in `brain.development.coherence_monitor._FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS` (case-insensitive); two invocations with identical inputs produce byte-identical output. `build_pledger_summary_text` rejects `None` / `int` / empty / non-printable / `COGITO_ID` `pattern_id`; `str` / `bool` / negative / over-cap `recurrence_count`; `None` / unknown-value `saturation_state_value`. The widened `_V1_EMITTED_SOURCES` set is observable through `build_rehearsal_provenance`: `REHEARSAL`, `PLEDGER_SUMMARY`, and (Phase 3.20) `COHMON_SUMMARY` all produce non-claim-clean bounded provenances; no `InternalEventSource` member is reserved at v0.28. `MODULE_PRODUCED_STRINGS` includes `PLEDGER_SUMMARY_TEXT_PREFIX == "pledger_summary"`, `FeedbackMode.OFF.value == "off"`, and `FeedbackMode.PATTERN_LEDGER.value == "pattern_ledger"`; no entry in `MODULE_PRODUCED_STRINGS` contains any forbidden non-claim term. | `brain/development/processing_window.py` | `internal_feedback_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |

### Phase 3.20 Coherence Feedback Bridge invariants

| I-CFBK-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.20 Coherence Feedback Bridge) | Architecture A + E: `OperatorSession._run_processing_window` fires a coherence-summary chunk after each rehearsal under `feedback_mode in {COHERENCE, PATTERN_AND_COHERENCE}`, producing `1 + 2 * N` (COHERENCE) or `1 + 3 * N` (PATTERN_AND_COHERENCE) stream chunks, deterministic recurrence accounting on cohmon-family and pledger-family second-order entries, kernel invariants green, zero real model calls. | After `OperatorSession(state=initial_state(), processing_window_size=N, feedback_mode=mode).dispatch(Command(STREAM_APPEND, payload=StreamAppendPayload(text=T)))` succeeds for `mode == FeedbackMode.COHERENCE`, the live `OperatorSession` has exactly `1 + 2 * N` chunks in `stream_history.chunks` whose `provenance` set partitions as `{"operator"} ∪ {f"internal_processing_window:{k}:rehearsal" for k in 1..N} ∪ {f"internal_processing_window:{k}:cohmon_summary" for k in 1..N}`; the `pattern_ledger.entries` tuple has length at least 2 (the seed entry plus at least one cohmon-family second-order entry whose `pattern_id` differs from the seed's `pattern_id`); the seed entry's `recurrence_count == min(STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MIN + N, STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX)`; the sum over all cohmon-family entries (entries whose evidence references at least one `cohmon_summary`-provenance chunk) of `(recurrence_count - STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MIN + 1)` equals exactly N (one observation per cohmon feedback chunk). For `mode == FeedbackMode.PATTERN_AND_COHERENCE`, the live session has exactly `1 + 3 * N` chunks (one operator + N rehearsal + N pledger_summary + N cohmon_summary); the pattern ledger has length at least 3 (seed + at least one pledger-family + at least one cohmon-family entry); the pledger and cohmon families are disjoint and both disjoint from the seed; the per-family observation sums each equal exactly N. For every mode, every entry's bounded constructor invariants hold; `assert_state_invariants(state)` remains green; two independent fresh `OperatorSession` instances with identical inputs and configuration produce bit-identical `pattern_ledger.entries` pattern_id tuples, bit-identical per-entry `recurrence_count` tuples, and bit-identical `growth_ledger.events` event_id tuples (determinism). At `processing_window_size == 0`, every `feedback_mode` is a strict no-op (one operator chunk; one Pattern Ledger entry at MIN). At `feedback_mode == FeedbackMode.OFF`, the path is bit-identical to the Phase 3.18 rehearsal-only behavior (no `pledger_summary` or `cohmon_summary` provenance appears). At `feedback_mode == FeedbackMode.PATTERN_LEDGER`, the path is bit-identical to the Phase 3.19 baseline (no `cohmon_summary` provenance appears). | `brain/development/processing_window.py`, `brain/ui/session.py` | `coherence_feedback_integration.py` | REQUIRED |

### Phase 3.24 Worldlet Feedback Bridge invariants

| I-WFDBK-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.24 Worldlet Feedback Bridge) | `build_worldlet_summary_text(*, state_id_value, step_index, object_count, attempt_count, response_count, accepted_count, pushback_count, last_reason_value)` is a pure deterministic helper that accepts only bounded primitives, validates `state_id_value` is a non-empty printable str of length `<= 64` (or sentinel `"absent"`), `step_index` int in `[0, _WORLDLET_SUMMARY_MAX_STEP_INDEX = 65535]`, each count int in `[0, _WORLDLET_SUMMARY_MAX_COUNT = 256]`, `last_reason_value` member of the closed set `{accepted, missing-target, rejected, target-unavailable, absent}`, cross-check `accepted_count + pushback_count <= response_count`, and returns the bounded printable template `"worldlet_summary state=<state> step=<n> objects=<n> attempts=<n> responses=<n> accepted=<n> pushback=<n> last_reason=<v>"` of length `<= WORLDLET_SUMMARY_TEXT_MAX_LEN = 240` and `<= STREAM_TEXT_MAX_LEN = 1024`; output contains no `COGITO_ID` and no forbidden non-claim term. | Two calls on the same inputs return byte-identical strings. The helper rejects every documented invalid input with a typed `ValueError`. | I-WFDBK-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.24 Worldlet Feedback Bridge) | The closed `FeedbackMode` `(str, Enum)` is widened to exactly the six values `{off, pattern_ledger, coherence, pattern_and_coherence, worldlet, pattern_coherence_worldlet}` (Phase 3.24 adds the trailing two); `validate_feedback_mode` accepts every member and rejects every other input with a typed `ValueError`. | `frozenset(m.value for m in FeedbackMode) == {"off","pattern_ledger","coherence","pattern_and_coherence","worldlet","pattern_coherence_worldlet"}`. `validate_feedback_mode(FeedbackMode.WORLDLET) is FeedbackMode.WORLDLET`. `validate_feedback_mode(FeedbackMode.PATTERN_COHERENCE_WORLDLET) is FeedbackMode.PATTERN_COHERENCE_WORLDLET`. `validate_feedback_mode("worldlet")` raises `ValueError`. `validate_feedback_mode(0)` / `True` / `None` each raise `ValueError`. | `brain/development/processing_window.py` | `worldlet_feedback_mode_validation.py` | REQUIRED |

| I-OSMO-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.25 Osmotic Learning Live Test) | `OsmoticExposureEvent` enforces bounded printable `text` (≤ 240), bounded printable `interaction_id` (≤ 64), 16-char hex `abstract_digest_hex16`, bounded printable `classification`, bounded printable `shape` (allowed to be empty), and non-claim-clean fields. | `OsmoticExposureEvent` rejects oversize / non-printable text, non-hex digest of the wrong length, oversize / non-printable classification or interaction_id, and any string containing a `_FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS` term. | I-OSMO-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.25 Osmotic Learning Live Test) | `OsmoticProbeTrial` enforces bounded printable `trial_id`, closed `OsmoticCondition`, bounded `exposure_texts` (≤ `OSMOTIC_MAX_EXPOSURES_PER_TRIAL = 8`), bounded printable `probe_text`, 16-char hex `expected_target_digest`, bounded printable `expected_target_shape`, bool `expected_prior_acquired` + `expected_transfer`. ### Phase 3.26 Active Hypothesis + Self-Directed Probe Loop invariants

| I-AHYP-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.26 Active Hypothesis + Self-Directed Probe Loop) | `ActiveHypothesisCandidate` and `ActiveProbeStep` enforce bounded printable fields, 16-char hex digests, closed-enum membership, and non-claim-clean strings. | `ActiveHypothesisCandidate` rejects oversize / non-printable `candidate_id`, `predicted_shape_name`, `predicted_shape`, `predicted_classification`; rejects non-`ProbeConstructionRule` `probe_construction_rule`; rejects non-`ActiveHypothesisStatus` `status`; rejects non-16-hex `predicted_digest_hex16`. `ActiveProbeStep` rejects probe text containing any forbidden direct-instruction term, rejects probe text containing the candidate's `predicted_digest_hex16` as a substring, rejects non-16-hex `probe_digest_hex16` / `predicted_digest_hex16` / `dispatch_trace_digest` / `reasoning_trace_digest`, rejects non-`ProbeOutcome` `outcome`, rejects oversize `reply_excerpt`. Two records with the same field values are equal. | `brain/development/active_hypothesis_probe.py` | `active_hypothesis_constructor.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-AHYP-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.26 Active Hypothesis + Self-Directed Probe Loop) | `ActiveHypothesisTrial`, `ActiveHypothesisResult`, and `ActiveHypothesisLiveTestReport` enforce bounded fields, the closed `AmbiguityCondition` / `TrialVerdict` membership, and the non-leakage discipline on operator inputs. | `ActiveHypothesisTrial` rejects oversize / non-printable `trial_id`, oversize `input_text`, non-printable input, input containing any `_FORBIDDEN_NON_CLAIM_TERMS` or `_FORBIDDEN_DIRECT_INSTRUCTION_TERMS` substring, non-`AmbiguityCondition` `condition`, out-of-range `expected_survivors_count` (must be in `[0, ACTIVE_HYPOTHESIS_MAX_CANDIDATES]`), non-string `expected_winner_id`, oversize `expected_winner_id`, non-bool `expected_no_hypothesis_survives` / `expected_second_visit_cache_hit`. `ActiveHypothesisResult` rejects oversize candidates tuple (> 8), oversize probe_steps tuple (> 8), non-16-hex `input_digest_hex16` / `learning_evidence_digest` / `reasoning_trace_digest`, non-tuple `dispatch_trace_digests`, non-`TrialVerdict` `verdict`. `ActiveHypothesisLiveTestReport` rejects oversize trials tuple (> 64), negative counts, non-16-hex `digest_hex16`. | `brain/development/active_hypothesis_probe.py` | `active_hypothesis_constructor.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-AHYP-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.26 Active Hypothesis + Self-Directed Probe Loop) | `enumerate_hypotheses(input_text)` is a pure deterministic function of the input's `(classification, token_count)`; it returns `()` when the input's classification is in `{empty, singleton, overlong, non-printable, too-many-tokens}` and otherwise returns the curated candidate tuple for that `(classification, token_count)` bucket bounded by `ACTIVE_HYPOTHESIS_MAX_CANDIDATES = 8`. Two invocations on the same input produce equal candidate tuples. | For every v1 trial input in `build_active_hypothesis_trials()`, `enumerate_hypotheses(input)` returns a tuple of length `<= 8`. Two consecutive invocations return tuples that are `==`. For `input_text == ""` and `input_text == "alpha"`, the result is `()`. For `input_text in {"red blue red", "red blue blue", "red red blue"}`, the result has length `4` and all four candidate ids are drawn from `{H_RENAME_S_ABA, H_RENAME_S_ABB, H_APPEND_POS0_S_ABCA, H_APPEND_NEW_S_ABCD}`. For `input_text == "red red"`, the result has length `4` and matches the `(repeated, 2)` bucket. | `brain/development/active_hypothesis_probe.py` | `active_hypothesis_enumerator.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-AHYP-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.26 Active Hypothesis + Self-Directed Probe Loop) | `select_safe_probe(input_text, candidate)` returns a bounded printable probe text whose body (a) does NOT contain `candidate.predicted_digest_hex16` as a substring, (b) does NOT contain `candidate.predicted_shape` as a substring, (c) contains none of the forbidden direct-instruction terms, (d) is the deterministic output of `construct_probe_text(input_text, candidate.probe_construction_rule)` (which never exceeds `ACTIVE_HYPOTHESIS_PROBE_MAX_LEN = 240`). | For every `(input, candidate)` pair generated by the v1 trial battery (10 trials, up to 4 candidates each), `select_safe_probe(input, candidate)` returns a bounded printable string with no forbidden direct-instruction substring (`learn`, `remember`, `pattern`, `classify`, `transfer`, `reuse`, `abab`, `abba`, `abcabc`, `structure`, `shape`, `imprint`, `osmotic`, `absorb`, `imbibe`, `intuition`, `hypothesis`, `candidate`, `probe`, `predict`, `falsify`, `survive`, `decide`, `infer`, `wonder`), no candidate `predicted_digest_hex16` substring, and no candidate `predicted_shape` substring. The function raises `ValueError` if any of these invariants would be violated. | `brain/development/active_hypothesis_probe.py` | `active_hypothesis_safe_probe.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-AHYP-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.26 Active Hypothesis + Self-Directed Probe Loop) | A `CONTROL_NO_AMBIGUITY` trial whose input has classification in `{empty, singleton}` produces an `ActiveHypothesisResult` with zero candidates, zero probe steps, zero survivors, empty winner_id, `no_hypothesis_survives == False`, `verdict == PASS`. | For v1 trial `T01_control_empty` (input `""`) and `T02_control_singleton` (input `"alpha"`), `run_active_hypothesis_trial(trial)` returns an `ActiveHypothesisResult` with `condition is AmbiguityCondition.CONTROL_NO_AMBIGUITY`, `len(candidates) == 0`, `len(probe_steps) == 0`, `survivors_count == 0`, `winner_id == ""`, `no_hypothesis_survives is False`, `verdict is TrialVerdict.PASS`. | `brain/development/active_hypothesis_probe.py` | `active_hypothesis_control.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-AHYP-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.26 Active Hypothesis + Self-Directed Probe Loop) | A `SINGLE_HYPOTHESIS_CONVERGES` trial enumerates a candidate set in which exactly one candidate's `predicted_digest_hex16` matches the digest of its constructed probe; that candidate is promoted to `SELECTED` and becomes the trial's winner. | For v1 trial `T03_single_aba` (input `"red blue red"`), `run_active_hypothesis_trial(trial)` returns `survivors_count == 1`, `winner_id == "H_RENAME_S_ABA"`, exactly one candidate with `status is ActiveHypothesisStatus.SELECTED`, and `false_positive is False`, `false_negative is False`, `verdict is TrialVerdict.PASS`. | I-AHYP-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.26 Active Hypothesis + Self-Directed Probe Loop) | A `MULTI_HYPOTHESIS_NARROWS` trial enumerates a candidate set in which two or more candidates' predicted digests match their constructed probe digests; the trial does NOT promote any candidate to `SELECTED` and the winner_id is empty. | For v1 trial `T05_multi_abc` (input `"red blue green"`), `run_active_hypothesis_trial(trial)` returns `survivors_count >= 2`, `winner_id == ""`, `no_hypothesis_survives is False`, `verdict is TrialVerdict.PASS`, and no candidate has `status is ActiveHypothesisStatus.SELECTED`. The Phase 3.11 Codex CLI runtime fixtures for I-LLMTOG-16 and I-LLMTOG-17 are live; `_PHASE3_11_PENDING_ROWS` is empty. The Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger row family (I-PLEDGER-01..16) is live via six new fixtures; `I-PLEDGER-17` (DEFERRED) and `I-PLEDGER-18` (NOT-EXERCISED) do not participate in I-CAT-01 coverage. The Phase 3.12c Coherence Monitor row family (I-COHMON-01..12) is live via six new fixtures; `I-COHMON-13` (DEFERRED) and `I-COHMON-14` (NOT-EXERCISED) do not participate in I-CAT-01 coverage. The Phase 3.13 Growth Ledger row family (I-GROW-01..20) is live via six new fixtures; `I-GROW-21` (DEFERRED) and `I-GROW-22` (NOT-EXERCISED) do not participate in I-CAT-01 coverage. The reclassified `I-PERSIST-16` row reuses the existing `persistence_static_audit.py` fixture and is registered in `brain/invariants.py` so the runner reports the row green from v0.19 onward without any change to the fixture file's audit body.

---

## Validation procedure

`python3 -m brain.invariants run` walks every `REQUIRED` row, loads each named fixture, and reports a structured pass/fail table. Catalog validation is complete when every gating row's row-id appears in the green column. The runner refuses to start if any `STRUCTURAL` builder check fails on construction (cogito sentinel, profile bounds, etc.) — those errors fire before any per-tick check. The runner also performs the import-graph audit for I-PCE-05 (`agency.py` never imports `pce.PCE`) and the I-CAT-01 coverage audit (every catalog REQUIRED/STRUCTURAL row has a registered check). Rows whose fixture column is `_meta` are enforced by the runner directly rather than by a fixture file; the runner registers a stub `@register` entry for each so they appear in the run summary.

---

## Pinned decisions

1. **Numeric core = `Fraction`.** `brain/tlica/`, `brain/fixtures/`, `brain/invariants.py` use `fractions.Fraction` throughout. `math.inf` (the single permitted float) represents Lean's `⊤` for empty-intersection `dInfShared`. The `rho()` constructor in `brain/tlica/builders.py` normalizes input at the I/O boundary; `TickRecord` may expose float views for display only.
2. **Three-way split:** `brain/tlica/builders.py` (construction-time preconditions, raises on invalid), `brain/validation.py` (reusable assertion helpers: `profile_equiv`, `is_in_unit_interval`, etc.), `brain/invariants.py` (catalog registry + runner). Dependency graph: `builders → validation`; `invariants → fixtures + validation`; `tick → builders + invariants`.

---

## Summary counts

- **REQUIRED v0.35 invariants:** 361
- **STRUCTURAL (constructor- or type-enforced, not per-tick asserted):** 99
- **NOT-EXERCISED row-level:** 14 (plus 5 modules covered at module-level in "Modules with no v0-required invariants")
- **DEFERRED row-level:** 15 (plus inherited deferrals table)
- **OBSERVED row-level:** 16 (recorded in run summary, not gating)

Total tabular entries: 505. v0.35 success is gated by the 361 REQUIRED rows + 99 STRUCTURAL rows (OBSERVED rows are logged but do not gate; the I-CAT-01 runner audit gates separately at startup).

---

## Build order (for Claude Code)

Do not start with `tick.py`. Build the object layer and invariant runner first, in this order:

1. `brain/tlica/profile.py`
2. `brain/tlica/msi.py`
3. `brain/tlica/ptcns.py`
4. `brain/tlica/builders.py`
5. `brain/validation.py`
6. `brain/invariants.py` (catalog registry + runner shell)
7. `brain/fixtures/minimal.py`
8. `brain/fixtures/cogito_invariants.py`

When those eight files pass their assigned invariants under `python -m brain.invariants run`, expand to the remaining modules and fixtures in the dependency order implied by the import graph (`preservation` → `project_map` → `pce` → `action_projection` → `agency` → `trajectory` → `affect`; `comparison/pointwise` parallel to those; `iboundary` after `ptcns`; `toce_core` independent of `brain/tlica/`).
